# VibeSpace

## Project Overview
A backend-agnostic web workspace for **coding agents** — manage many concurrent agent CLI sessions with a tiling window manager, file explorer, and code editor. Each backend (Claude Code, Codex, …) is driven through a `BackendAdapter` (`src/adapters/`); the UI, window manager, chat view, and session layer stay backend-neutral. Sessions run via native agent CLIs inside **dtach** for persistence across server restarts. (Project was "Claude Code WebUI" before the 2026-06-22 rename to VibeSpace — references to the `claude`/Claude Code CLI tool itself are unchanged.)

## How to Build and Run
```bash
# One-line install (checks deps, clones, builds):
curl -fsSL https://raw.githubusercontent.com/ProblemFactory/vibespace/master/install.sh | bash

# Or manually:
npm install
npm run build   # esbuild bundles src/client.js → public/bundle.js (~1.8MB)
node server.js  # starts on port 3456 (or PORT env var)
# ./run.sh      # supervised: build once, then respawn on exit (survives an OOM kill)

# PRODUCTION (this machine runs it this way since 2.73.0): systemd USER service
./scripts/install-service.sh        # installs+enables ~/.config/systemd/user/vibespace.service (linger on)
systemctl --user restart vibespace  # THE way to restart after a build — do NOT kill+nohup by hand
./scripts/update.sh                 # pull+install+build+restart in one step (⚙ → Update VibeSpace… runs this in a shell terminal; dtach sessions survive)
journalctl --user -u vibespace -f   # logs (no more /tmp/vibespace-server.log)
# Unit: Restart=always/RestartSec=5 (survives OOM/crash — verified via SIGKILL), OOMScoreAdjust=-500,
# StartLimitIntervalSec=0 (retries forever while the NFS workspace mounts late), **KillMode=process**
# (CRITICAL — the default control-group KillMode killed every dtach session spawned AFTER the service
# migration on each restart, while pre-migration sessions survived; real incident, one session died on
# every restart. Only the node main process may be killed on stop), and baked PATH (node dir +
# ~/.local/bin — systemd's minimal env broke every CLI spawn; real incident). The service does NOT
# build — build at deploy, then restart. dtach sessions survive restarts by design.
```

## Architecture

### Stack
- **Backend**: Node.js + Express + WebSocket (`ws`) + `node-pty` + dtach
- **Frontend**: Vanilla JS (ES modules) bundled with esbuild, xterm.js for terminals, CodeMirror 6 for editor
- **Session persistence**: dtach — claude processes run in dtach sessions, survive server restarts
- **Data persistence**: `data/layouts.json`, `data/session-meta/*.json`, `data/sockets/cw-*`

### Data Flow
```
Terminal mode:
  Browser (xterm.js) ←→ WebSocket ←→ node-pty (dtach -a) ←→ dtach socket ←→ pty-wrapper.js ←→ claude CLI
                                                                                  ↓
                                                                            buffer file (raw PTY)

Chat mode:
  Browser (ChatView) ←→ WebSocket (msg create/edit/meta) ←→ MessageManager ←→ server ←→ chat-wrapper.js ←→ claude --stream-json
                                                                   ↓
                                                          BackendAdapter (swappable)
```

## File Structure
```
server.js              — Express server bootstrap, PTY/dtach infrastructure, session restore (~2700 lines)
editor-helper.sh       — Ctrl+G editor helper (overwritten by server on startup)
data/bin/code          — Fake "code" script for Ctrl+G (generated by server)
data/bin/pty-wrapper.js — PTY wrapper for terminal mode (runs inside dtach, survives server restarts)
data/bin/vibespace-hook.mjs — Dual-harness hook (SessionStart→task context OR a baseline tools intro for no-task sessions, UserPromptSubmit→first-prompt context + status-override notices + per-turn micro-reminder, Stop→bookkeeping nudge (2.79.0, CLAUDE-ONLY registration): calls GET /api/agent/stop-check and emits {decision:'block', reason} when the server says the board state is stale — the agent gets ONE follow-up mini-turn to set status/mirror asks/log progress, gated by stop_hook_active (never loops), server-side staleness+cooldown thresholds (agents.stopNudgeStaleMinutes/CooldownMinutes, defaults 10/30min, clamped 1-240/2-720 — 2.89.0; an EXPLICIT 0 = every-stop mode: 0 stale = always stale, 0 cooldown = none — 2.210.0 user request; stop_hook_active/nudgeTurnActive still cap it at ONE mini-turn per user turn); codex's equivalent rides codex-chat-wrapper's turn/completed (maybeStopNudge → synthetic <vibespace-reminder> turn, nudgeTurnActive guard) since the app-server has no blockable Stop in JSON-RPC mode; generated at startup; env-gated no-op only when VIBESPACE_API/TOKEN are absent — a MISSING VIBESPACE_TASK_ID no longer no-ops (2.38.0), so any VibeSpace session still learns `vibespace-status`; emits ONLY nested hookSpecificOutput). Registered idempotently for BOTH events in ~/.claude/settings.json + ~/.codex/hooks.json by ensureAgentHooks — only the vibespace entry is ever touched. **INTEGRATION MASTER SWITCH (2.190.0, settings category "Integration"): `agents.vibespaceIntegration` default ON; OFF = the model gets a pristine CLI. SCOPE = AGENT-VISIBLE integration ONLY (2.190.1, user decision): model-invisible plumbing is EXEMPT — the usage statusline, billing/account env, Ctrl+G editor, keeper transport all keep working either way. PER-FEATURE toggles under it (2.211.0, user request '注入context但不给ask/progress'): `agents.contextInjection` (group payloads/diffs; per-group injectContext stays the finer grain) + `agents.toolStatus`/`toolAsk`/`toolTask` — a disabled tool is neither TAUGHT (sessionToolsIntro()/renderContext's _toolsSectionParts/per-turn reminder/stop-nudge steps all compose from enabledTools(); teaching a refusing command trains dead ends) nor SERVED (its write endpoints 403 with skip-and-continue-do-not-retry guidance); toolStatus off also silences the stop-check arbiter (it is keyed on status staleness); contextInjection off falls back to the baseline tools intro; reads (GET /api/agent/task = `vibespace-task show`) stay governed by the master, not toolTask. Route smoke: scripts/test-tool-toggles.mjs (21 asserts).** Hook entries stripped live on toggle (persistence writeSettings' `onSettingsWrite` callback → stripAgentHookEntries; boot re-checks the setting so a flip-while-down converges; the boot ensureAgentHooks call is DEFERRED until after setupPersistence so the setting is readable), new spawns get NO VIBESPACE_API/tools-PATH/remote-prelude (keeper still ships; VIBESPACE_SESSION_TOKEN stays for Ctrl+G editor auth, inert alone since every consumer guards on api+token), and agent-routes gates every model-visible CONTENT response for pre-toggle sessions too: the three deliveries return empty (prompt-context also consumes-and-DROPS pending status-override notices — deferring them injected stale reminders on re-enable) and GET /api/agent/task 403s (it returns the same steering substance; `vibespace-task show` must not bypass the pristine state) while WRITE endpoints stay live. Both Install routes (local /api/agent-hooks/install AND host /api/hosts/:id/agent-tools/install) refuse while OFF; the Manage-Agents host row shows the residue + keeps Remove as cleanup. Dial spawns drop the `$HOME/.vibespace/bin` PATH segment too (leftover tools from earlier ON spawns must not be name-resolvable). Distinct from the data/.agent-hooks-optout marker (manual Manage-Agents Remove) — the setting never writes the marker, and re-enable does NOT override it. E2E: scripts/test-integration-toggle.mjs. vibespace-hook-register.mjs = self-locating installer distributed to remote hosts (P3); its `--uninstall` mode (2.129.0) strips ONLY our entry from the remote configs (foreign hooks untouched) — the Manage-Agents remote Remove path
data/bin/vibespace-task — Agent task-reporting CLI (STATIC tracked file, not generated — inline template-in-template escaping was unmaintainable): show [--full]/progress "summary" [--detail]/backlog/backlog-add/backlog-done/backlog-drop → /api/agent/task* (scoped to the session's own context task). **progress SUCCESS OUTPUT reminds the agent (2.210.0, the vibespace-ask 2.111.21 pattern): the activity log is agent-facing — deliverables (URLs/paths/results) must ALSO go in the chat reply (real pattern: agent logged a URL via progress and ended the turn without saying it).** **CHECKLIST REMOVED (2.121.0, user decision):** `plan-check/plan-uncheck/plan-add` are gone — a group-level list of agent WORK ITEMS never made sense (those live at the SESSION level = the agent's own todo list, surfaced as the card's Steps). The subcommands now print a redirect; `/api/agent/task-plan` answers old CLI copies (remote hosts) with 410 + guidance; stored `plan` arrays stay DORMANT in data/task-groups.json (never rendered/written; update() ignores plan patches; config-bundle import passes them through). **BACKLOG ADDED (2.122.0; CLAIM MODEL 2.123.0 — a DIFFERENT concept on the same shelf):** the group's PARKING LOT for NON-immediate items (deferred user decisions, "later" work; item = {**id: stable `B-xxxx`**, text, detail?, status open|done|dropped, **claimedBy: [session keys]**, addedBy/At, resolvedBy/At}); agents park via `backlog-add` when the user defers something (parking AUTO-CLAIMS for the caller) and are taught to NEVER start parked items unasked. Refs everywhere = id / 1-based OPEN-list index / unique substring; **the id travels** — the user copies it from the viewer and hands it to ANY member agent ("看一下 backlog B-ab12"), which runs `backlog <id>` (full item view, works on resolved items) and `backlog-claim <id>`. **INJECTION IS SUMMARY-ONLY + TARGETED (user directives): the hook never dumps the backlog** — renderContext gets `sessionKey` and emits a compact reminder block ONLY for open items THAT session CLAIMED (+ a one-line "N open — `vibespace-task backlog`" pointer otherwise); change events (PARKED/RESOLVED/DROPPED/CLAIMED/UNCLAIMED/reworded/REMOVED) ride the diff updates but reach ONLY sessions that created or claimed the item — diff matching is by the stable id (text edit ⇒ "reworded", not REMOVED+NEW). TASK.md/`show` carry the full open list with ids+claimants. One-time seed: dormant plan's unchecked items → open backlog items; id + creator-auto-claim backfill for pre-2.123.0 items (constructor, idempotent). **SUMMARY+DETAIL split (2.69.0):** progress entries carry a one-line `note` (what everyone sees inline — board rows, injected context marked `†`) + optional `detail` (≤6000 chars; TASK.md renders it as an indented blockquote, `show --full` prints it, the board's Activity rows expand on click) — this keeps the byte-budgeted injection dense without losing information. session-status records gained the same: `reason` = one-liner on chips, `detail` (≤2000) shown in Session Properties + `vibespace-status show`
data/bin/vibespace-ask — Agent CLI for the GLOBAL USER-TODO inbox (2.65.0, STATIC tracked): files items the USER must act on (decision/input/review) → POST /api/agent/user-todo (vsst_ scoped to own session). `"text" [--detail] [--urgency]` / list / resolve <id|text>; `help|-h|--help` and any flag-looking first arg print usage instead of filing (2.76.0 — a real agent filed the literal item "--help"); idempotent re-file by same text; the SUCCESS OUTPUT reminds the agent (2.111.21) that the inbox is only a notification mirror — the full content must ALSO go in the chat reply (real pattern: agents filed and ended the turn silently). **Semantics (2.76.1, user directive): MIRROR every chat question** — whenever an agent asks the user anything in chat / ends a turn waiting on them / sets needs-input|blocked|review, it must ALSO file the item (the user is often not watching that window), and the moment the user answers ANYWHERE (chat counts) the agent resolves it itself — taught in all three surfaces (SESSION_TOOLS_INTRO, renderContext tools section, the CLI's own usage text); taught in SESSION_TOOLS_INTRO + renderContext; distributed to remote hosts like the other tools
data/bin/vibespace-status — Agent status tool (GENERATED at startup like data/bin/code — NEVER git-track it: tracking it dirtied the tree every boot and blocked `git pull --ff-only` in self-update (real incident 2.111.26); gitignored (NOTE: .gitignore has NO inline comments — a `path  # comment` line becomes the whole pattern and never matches, which silently re-tracked it once) and update.sh resets any regenerated tracked data/bin file before pulling. GENERATOR-TEMPLATE GOTCHA (P0 2.111.29): a shell example ending a single-quoted JS template string with `\\` rendered as `\'` → escaped the closing quote → every generated file was a SyntaxError and the whole CLI crashed on 2.111.24-28 — never end a JS template string with a bare backslash. WAITING STATES REQUIRE COMPLETE REASONS (2.111.24): blocked/needs-input/review need BOTH --reason (board chip) AND --detail (full context) — CLI pre-flight (show-lookup grace for same-state urgency tweaks) + agent-route both reject otherwise; done/working exempt; setting a waiting state prints a point-of-use reminder to also say it in chat + mirror via vibespace-ask)
data/bin/vibespace-usage — PASSIVE usage capture (STATIC tracked file, not generated; 2.60.0). A `statusLine` hook injected via `--settings` into LOCAL CLAUDE TERMINAL sessions only (2.62.0: the ws-handler injection is gated `backend==='claude'` — only the claude CLI understands `--settings`; un-gated it rode on `zsh -l` and codex spawns too, making every shell terminal (incl. the Manage-Agents Update/Login helpers) and local codex terminal exit instantly as "terminated"; NOT gated by the Integration master switch — 2.190.1 user decision: the switch scopes to AGENT-VISIBLE integration only, and the statusline is model-invisible plumbing) — the CLI feeds it the payload's `rate_limits` (5h/7d used_percentage+reset, "only after first API response" — and NOTHING else: model-scoped buckets like the Fable weekly cap are NOT in the statusline payload, verified vs the 2.1.206 payload builder) which it writes to data/usage-cache/<accountKey>.json (throttle 8s; **PRESERVES `scopedWeekly`/`scopedFetchedAt` from the existing file** — 2.70.0, clobbering them to [] every write is what made Fable vanish from the quota popup) + passes through the user's own statusline. Also harvests `model.id` → data/usage-cache/__models__.json (passive model discovery). ZERO Anthropic calls — this is why VibeSpace makes no background /api/oauth/usage poll by default (that off-CLI fixed-cadence sub-token call is the #1 ban trigger — see §ban-safety on accounts.js). Chat/stream-json has no statusline → those accounts show last-known.
data/bin/chat-wrapper.js — Chat wrapper for stream-json mode (runs inside dtach, parses JSON lines)
data/bin/codex-chat-wrapper.js — Codex chat wrapper (JSON-RPC protocol, thread management)
data/bin/vibespace-usage-scan — REMOTE-side usage ledger scanner (2.127.0, STATIC tracked; shipped over ssh stdin per harvest, never argv): walks the host's ~/.claude/projects with remote byte cursors (~/.vibespace/usage-cursor.json), emits per-request NDJSON events (claude-only v1); cursor persists ONLY after stdout fully flushed (interrupted transfer ⇒ re-emit, rid-dedup absorbs). Harvest chain: hosts.harvestUsage (15min/host throttle) → usageHistory.ingestRemoteEvents (acct=<hostId>, atype='host', billing 'remote-host', aname=host name; rid namespaced `h:<id>:`; host events EXEMPT from _loadEvents re-attribution — the local attribution log would re-bucket them to global) → POST /api/usage-stats/harvest-hosts (kicked on Usage-window open, reload on added>0). Quota side: /api/usage/refresh {host} = on-demand ⟳ with hosts.readRemoteOAuth (READ-ONLY remote token peek, never refresh, §ban-safety) → usage-cache/host-<id>.json → GET /api/usage `hosts` field (every configured host listed) → popup "Remote hosts" section (bars + per-host ⟳, class usage-host-refresh)
data/bin/vibespace-remote-keeper — REMOTE-side persistence for remote CHAT sessions (2.124.0, STATIC tracked; distributed to remote ~/.vibespace/bin with the other tools): claude runs setsid-DETACHED on the host under a keeper daemon (stdout→buffer file, stdin←unix socket) so an ssh drop kills only the pipe; the local chat-wrapper reattaches with a byte offset (`run <sid> <offset> -- cmd`; stdout carries ONLY raw buffer bytes — diagnostics on stderr), `_remote_exit` sentinel = claude really ended (run never restarts an exited sid); stop mode = the kill path. See the 远程session稳定性 bullet + scripts/test-remote-keeper.mjs
data/sockets/cw-*      — dtach socket files (session anchors)
data/session-buffers/  — Per-session output buffer files (written by pty-wrapper)
data/session-meta/     — Per-session metadata JSON
data/layouts.json      — Persisted layouts and autosave state
data/drafts.json       — Chat input drafts (SyncStore, versioned, multi-client synced)
data/settings-sync.json — Settings SyncStore (future migration target)
src/
  client.js            — Entry point (2 lines): imports App and initializes
  ws-handler.js        — WebSocket protocol handler (all WS message cases, extracted from server.js)
  sync-store.js        — SyncStore class (versioned state sync with diff broadcast)
  session-store.js     — SessionMessages + JSONL parsing + session discovery helpers. **Merge is POSITION-PRESERVING (2.74.0):** surviving buffer records interleave at their true chronological spot (anchor = jsonl index of the last buffer record that deduped; a rotated buffer's unmatched head anchors just before the first match) instead of all appending at the end — end-append made an EARLIER turn's stream-json-only `result` replay AFTER a still-running tool_use, flushing the live pending tool card to ✗ Interrupted on every server restart (real report), and scrambled turn boundaries in the replay
  message-manager.js   — MessageManager (Claude stream-json → normalized messages with stable IDs). **convertHistory is per-record isolated + _historyLoaded set AFTER successful rebuild (2.89.2)** — a single throwing record amputated every restart-rebuilt view at that point and the flag-before-work made it permanent (real fleet-wide incident: the 2.80.0 `output`→`raw.output` hook-card typo threw on every buffered hook_response; live path swallowed it per-line so it hid for 9 releases). **queued_command attachments = mid-turn user messages (2.88.0)**: the JSONL's ONLY record of a message sent while the agent works — normalized into a real user message (typed-flagged, echo-deduped by exact text vs the last 12) or the user's words vanish from every JSONL-rebuilt history (restart/resume/view-only; real incident, 211 records). msg.typed (promptSource/_fromWebui) beats notification text-shape in renderUserMsg; msg.synthetic (isSynthetic) forces it
  codex-message-manager.js — CodexMessageManager (Codex JSON-RPC → normalized messages)
  codex-session-store.js — Codex session discovery (thread listing, JSONL parsing, forkedFrom chain merge)
  normalizers.js       — createMessageManager(backend, id) factory for backend-agnostic normalization
  mounts.js            — MountManager (rclone mounts, MULTI-SOURCE: typed records s3/drive/onedrive/gmail/webdav/sftp/vibespace/rclone via _rcloneFor; detached + boot adoption; one-click rclone install (data/bin, pinned 1.65.2); guided Google Drive OAuth; rclone.conf import; per-mount S3 share minting mc→STS; NATIVE cephfs type (2.109.1, all-flash deployment storage — kernel `sudo mount -t ceph`, per-user quota, env-provisioned My storage VIBESPACE_CEPHFS_* replaces S3, no CSI); flat-connections model — no special my-storage slot, env auto-migrates to a normal mount. **SUBMOUNT model (2.108.0→2.108.2, user-refined twice): ANY top-level storage record can hold submounts — children reference the parent via `parentId` + their own path fields (`remote:path`) and resolve connection through `_connOf()` at use time (addChild allows any non-child parent; no nesting). `kind:'credential'` now means CREDENTIAL-ONLY (root unmountable — bucket-scoped token): UI shows a key ICON in place of the status dot (no text badge, user directive) and NO Connect action; mount() auto-heals kind on a later successful root probe — refreshing the credential's token/keys heals every child (update() bounces mounted children). A credential itself mounts fine when its token can list the remote root (GDrive, account-wide keys); mount() AUTO-DETECTS bucket-scoped tokens (pathless s3-family + root-list probe AccessDenied → convert to credential + guidance) because the fuse mount otherwise "succeeds" and EIOs on every IO (the FishR2 trap — real bucket was `example-prod-data`; S3 names are lowercase). AccessDenied WITH a path fails fast pre-mount with a check-the-bucket-name error (v2Auth probe extension; v2Auth stays undefined so a fixed path re-probes). addChild/convert/remove-guarded; export re-links children by parent NAME. Drive re-auth: startDriveAuthForMount(id) runs the guided OAuth with the mount's own client creds, applyDriveToken() writes back + reconnects children — the invalid_grant recovery path. Non-env mounts expose ALL connection params in the edit dialog PREFILLED with their real current values, SECRETS INCLUDED (2.108.8, user directive: no more blank "=default" fields — `_showEditMountDialog` fetches the decrypted config via `GET /api/mounts/:id/config`/`config()` and fills every input, keys/tokens/passwords/rclone params too; single-user instance, inputs stay type=text); save is a DIFF — a field is sent only when it changed from the fetched original (unchanged secrets aren't needlessly re-encrypted; server ignores an emptied secret so clearing one is a no-op there), an emptied rclone per-param row removes it. Only my-storage locks connection fields (edit shows name+mountpoint only; `config()` returns `{envLocked:true}` with no secrets). **HUNG-MOUNT DEFENSE (2.108.3, real outage)**: a fuse mount to an unreachable backend (home-LAN SMB host from a datacenter pod) hangs every IO — node's libuv THREADPOOL fills with stuck fs ops and the whole server stops answering while the event loop stays idle (ep_poll; /login 130s → readiness dead → pod out of Service). mount() runs a post-mount child-process `ls` probe (6s guard; error-exit=responsive, only a STUCK child trips) and startHealthWatchdog() sweeps every mounted record (60s + 15s-after-boot, covers boot-ADOPTED mounts that skip mount()) — hang ⇒ lazy unmount + `_killMountDaemon` (exact /proc cmdline argv match — a wedged rclone survives fusermount -uz) + desired=unmounted persisted + row error. Never probe mountpoints with node fs — child processes only. 2.108.4: pathBlocked() circuit breaker — mount() blocks the root for the WHOLE connect window and hang-detection blocks 90s; a files.js router middleware fails every op under a blocked root fast with 503 (an open explorer window otherwise stuffs the pool during the probe window — real follow-up incident); UV_THREADPOOL_SIZE=32 at the top of server.js (before any pool-touching require). **2.109.0 STRUCTURAL FIX: src/safe-fs.js worker_threads pool** — every LOCAL user-path fs op in routes/files.js runs in a worker with its OWN libuv pool + per-op deadline + kill/respawn (path resolution/traversal stay in main; worker executes the resolved absolute path only; ?host= untouched; app.locals.safeFs wired in server.js, inline fallback if the pool fails). Revoked/expired share SURFACING: _probeMountpoint is 3-state (ok/error/hung) + _probeBackendAccess (uncached rclone lsf re-auth, gated to _revocable = imported/vibespace/expiring) catches a 401/403 that a cache-served mountpoint ls hides → row shows "connected but every file errors" (clears on re-grant). 2.108.5 SELF-MOUNT GUARD: a vibespace-bridge record whose bearer token exists in OUR OWN MountTokens store points back at this instance — fuse→HTTP→self deadlocks the threadpool (real incident); refused at add/import/mount via mounts.selfTokenCheck = mountTokens.has(raw) (no lastUsedAt bump)**. **DIRECT CEPHFS SUBTREE SHARING (2.111.7): sharing a folder from a cephfs My-storage mount calls an in-cluster minter (env VIBESPACE_CEPHMINT_URL/_TOKEN) to mint a PATH-SCOPED cephx key (`ceph fs authorize <fs> client.vibespace-share-<rand> <path> <r|rw>`) and emits a `vibespace-cephmount:v1:<b64>` link; import → a normal `cephfs` mount that KERNEL-mounts the subtree directly (full flash bandwidth, no WebDAV relay). Key scoped to exactly the subpath (mds allow r path=…), recorded in `_state.shares` (kind:cephmount), revoke deletes it cluster-side. Env-gated — absent the minter, sharing falls back to the WebDAV bridge; cross-cluster/external always uses the bridge. mintCephShare/parseCephMountLink/revoke path in mounts.js; canCephShare in list(); `_showCephShareDialog` UI. Helm: storage.existingClaim (mount a pre-made PVC — the home-SC migration lever) + cephMint.{url,token}.** **2.110.0 HARDENING (user directive 最稳定+性能最好+自动恢复): every rclone mount runs `--vfs-cache-mode full` with a PERSISTENT per-mount cache dir (data/vfs-cache/<id>, root overridable VIBESPACE_VFS_CACHE_DIR; setting mounts.vfsCacheMaxSizeGB default 10G) — dirty writes survive a daemon crash and resume uploading on remount (verified live: SIGKILL 0.5s post-write → auto-remount → object lands); bounded IO (--timeout 60s --contimeout 15s + retries) so flaky backends error instead of hanging; new flags gated via _rcloneHasFlag (old system rclone falls back to writes mode). AUTO-RECONNECT supervision: desired now ONLY reflects user intent — internal teardowns (hang defense) keep desired=mounted and _healthSweep's dead-mount branch remounts with backoff 1→2→5→10min (_maybeAutoRemount; _noteReconnectBackoff), auth-class errors (denied/revoked/expired/AccessDenied…) excluded from retry so the actionable message survives; unmount(id,{internal:true}) is the internal teardown that doesn't rewrite intent; mount() is wrapped by a _connecting guard (one connect in flight per record). rcloneBin() NFS trap: executing the 57MB binary from a network FS demand-pages it per exec (~22s measured) — _fastBin copies it once to ~/.cache/vibespace keyed by size+mtime (22s→0.03s), detection via /proc/mounts longest-prefix fstype**)
  gmail-sync.js        — GmailSync (2.134.0, backlog B-64db): Gmail-as-a-folder — a 'gmail' mount = local dir of .eml files synced READ-ONLY from the Gmail API (GYB-style; NOT FUSE). Own loopback OAuth for gmail.readonly (rclone authorize is drive-only; same guided UX incl. remote paste-back); seed = STREAMING + CHECKPOINTED (2.136.1-4): each page downloaded then a CROSS-RESTART cursor persisted — a DATE (`state.seedOldestMs` → `before:<sec>`), NOT the messages.list pageToken (pageToken is only stable within one run; new mail between runs shifts/expires it and silently skips OLD mail the incremental never back-fills — real user catch). historyId anchored at seed START (covers mail arriving during a long seed). Total for the N/total bar comes cheaply from users.getProfile `messagesTotal` (whole mailbox) or labels.get `messagesTotal` (label filter), persisted as `state.seedTotal` (free-text query → indeterminate). Progress broadcasts throttle (indeterminate 2.5s — a fast cadence rebuilt the card and restarted the bar animation, stuttering it 'in the first third'; the bar is a symmetric pulse so a mid-anim rebuild is invisible). Incremental via history.list (404 = expired → reseed; dir tree IS the dedup index — msg id in filename tail, _seenIds recurses one date/label dir level), messages.get?format=raw → base64url → .eml (atomic tmp+rename, RFC2047-decoded subject slug in name). Client id/secret from VIBESPACE_GDRIVE_CLIENTS presets (they carry gmail scope) or custom — NO built-in fallback. mounts.js integration: isMounted=worker alive, health sweep skips fuse probing (dead worker → auto-restart), unmount stops worker but keeps files (it's the archive), mode forced ro. Viewer: src/lib/eml.js (dependency-free browser-safe MIME parser, 41-case test) + file-viewer _renderEml (header card, text/html toggle, html in sandbox="" iframe, attachment blob downloads). **2.151.0 incremental-freeze fix (real 3h hang):** history.list lists ADDED ids that can be deleted by fetch time (spam auto-purge; guaranteed with includeSpamTrash) — the per-message 404 failed the whole pass and the cursor only advances after a COMPLETE pass ⇒ every 120s retry re-listed + re-404'd the same dead id forever. _writeGone404 skips gone messages (both paths); all API/token fetches bounded (AbortSignal.timeout 60s/30s) so a wedged socket errors into the backoff. Tests: scripts/test-gmail-sync.mjs (mock API e2e incl the dead-id regression), scripts/test-eml.mjs
  agentd/               — CS refactor (B-5052) machine agent — ALL milestones' protocol+device side COMPLETE and acceptance-tested (2.140.0–2.146.0; docs/design-remote-cs.md + M0 addendum + milestone record). THREE flags, DEFAULT ON since 2.158.0 (CS graduation — local=device#0; automatic legacy fallback preserved). **ONE MACHINE MODEL since 2.160.0 (B-f3e8, resolves the user's 2026-07-15 insight that row inconsistencies = two underlying concepts): a machine is a host record, transport ∈ {ssh(absent), dial}** — the pairing credential lives ON the dial record (`dialTokenHash`, redacted from list(), migrated ONCE from dial-tokens.json via hosts.migrateDialTokenFile → `.migrated`; LOSSLESS is load-bearing: in-field daemons hold the raw tokens); roster/test/unpair = /api/hosts + POST /api/hosts/:id/test (hosts.test dial branch = mux runCmd probe) + DELETE /api/hosts/:id (server unpairDialDevice: mounts+token-file+live-stream teardown); /api/agentd/devices is GONE; `hosts-updated` broadcasts on pair/unpair/dial-in/out; hosts.dirComplete rides the device link (dial machines get real remote autocomplete); sidebar has ONE _buildHostRow for all transports + a 'This machine' local row (local=device#0 made visible). The flags: `agentd.sessions` (M1: local sessions run in the daemon — dtach attach inside agentd, survives server restarts), `agentd.remoteSessions` (M2: remote chat = persistent pipe session in the remote daemon via the vibespace-agentd-attach bridge, keeper-run-identical contract so chat-wrapper is untouched; auto install/refresh at spawn), `agentd.dataPlane` (M3 switchovers: RemoteFs fs ops / discovery raw-facts synthesized into the ssh-script line format→UNCHANGED parser / transcript INCREMENTAL slab sync (append-only delta via read-range — no more whole-file remote-jsonl pulls) / usage harvest via run-stream; per-path ssh fallback; hosts.device(id) = per-host DeviceManager registry). mux.js = length-prefixed binary mux (chan0 JSON control + credit-flow-controlled byte channels; data() SPLITS at the window — all-or-nothing starved big writes; zero deps, shared by daemon+server = invariant #3). **CONTROL-OVERTAKE INVARIANT (2.187.0, real incident): chan0 control is credit-EXEMPT, so a completion marker (fs-done/stream-exit) OVERTAKES data still queued behind the 256KB window — any "resolve on the done marker" consumer truncates big transfers to exactly INITIAL_WINDOW bytes.** fsReadRange/runStream are COUNT-GATED (resolve when the counted bytes landed; daemon reports `sent`, run-stream exits on 'close' not 'exit', both pace under window pressure via onWritable); the incident: a 45MB remote transcript cached as a 256KB prefix stamped complete → permanently ancient chat history (fetchSessionJsonl now also refuses to stamp meta for bytes not received + caps on FETCHED delta not total size; **2.188.1: cache-valid additionally requires the cached FILE to hold meta.size bytes — a pre-fix stump over a STOPPED transcript passed size/mtime forever since the self-heal only fired on remote-file change**). Any NEW byte-channel consumer must gate on a byte count, never on a control-channel done. Test: scripts/test-agentd-bigread.mjs. agentd.js = daemon (flock singleton, setsid, 0700 unix socket, multi-server, vsht_ hello auth, self-upgrade→versioned dir→re-exec (2.185.2: the re-exec PRESERVES the original argv via reExecArgv — dropping `--dial/--dial-token` re-exec'd a dial device into LISTEN mode and wedged the link behind the singleton, the walter-class 'device goes offline after updates' root cause); pipe-sessions = keeper semantics in-daemon (setsid child + buffer/fifo + offset reattach + sentinel + drain-only-never-respawn); **pipe-child identity is exec-PROOF startTime, never cmdline (2.184.1, real lengyue outage: chat children spawn as `sh -lc '… exec env … claude'` so cmdline loses argv0 — every daemon upgrade re-exec then misjudged the live claude as a recycled pid, synthesized a crash sentinel (session died, claude orphaned) AND made kill-pipe-session a no-op; adopted children additionally get a liveness watcher because a non-child can't be wait()ed — no watcher meant no exit sentinel ever; test-agentd-adopt.mjs guards both)**; fs-op incl read-range byte-chan slab; discovery snapshot w/ tailIds/headCwd/userLines enrichment + fs.watch dirty push; run-cmd (argv-only bounded); run-stream (unbounded stdout on byte chan); tcp-connect (loopback only = VNC bridge shape); **serve-folder (2.150.0; WEBDAV since 2.151.0, device-folder-mount): a minimal in-daemon read-only WebDAV subset (OPTIONS/PROPFIND Depth 0-1/HEAD/GET+Range; zero deps, mirrors src/webdav.js) bound to 127.0.0.1 that rclone `webdav`-mounts via tcp-connect (src/device-mount.js) — the plain-`http` backend was the 2.150.0 stall: it requests a fixed 128MB range per read then waits ~6s on the keep-alive connection after the clamped 206; webdav requests sane ranges and reads in ~7ms (verified). GOTCHAS: clamp ranged end to size-1 (rclone asks 128M ranges → clamp or truncated EIO); the SERVER-side bridge net.createServer MUST be `{allowHalfOpen:true}` + attach the data listener BEFORE `await tcpForward` (curl/rclone half-close a GET's write side + write-then-read, both lose bytes otherwise); NEVER do sync fs/exec on a device mountpoint from the process hosting the bridge — the blocked event loop can't pump the tunnel, the FUSE read never completes, SELF-DEADLOCK (the acceptance test hung itself this way for a whole debug cycle; a dir `ls` still 'works' off rclone's dir-cache, which hides it; test IO now runs in async children w/ watchdog — production safe by construction: bridge in the server, reads from other processes/safe-fs workers). Still not a MountManager UI type (next step). dial-in device consumption = DeviceManager `stream` transport + server deviceForDial(id) wrapping a dialed-in ws stream — **deviceForDial NEVER reuses a stop()ed DeviceManager (2.169.0, real walter outage: hours of phantom-offline against a healthy dialed-in Mac): stop() is terminal (_connectLoop throws 'stopped' forever), so a stopped dm is evicted like a stale stream and a failed connect() never stays cached; any new dm.stop() caller must not leave the object in agentdDialDevices**. Dial chat TERMINATE kills the device-side claude via the daemon's `kill-pipe-session` (client killPipeSession) + rm's the session token over the device link — the ssh-only teardown threw for dial and silently orphaned claude (double-JSONL-writer class). Pairing commands render `/api/device-dial`; `/api/agentd-dial` is a PERMANENT alias (in-field daemons hold it in dial.json); env `VIBESPACE_DEVICE_ROOT` preferred, `VIBESPACE_AGENTD_ROOT` honored forever. **RE-PAIR / IDENTITY ROTATION (2.170.0, the walter-incident class): the daemon re-reads dial.json on EVERY dial attempt and the host-token file on EVERY hello — a re-pair heals a RUNNING daemon within one retry; never cache either at startup (the cached identity dialed a dead pairing forever while the singleton blocked its replacement + launchd respawn-spammed). The installer replaces a running same-root daemon (cmdline-verified kill); macOS singleton verifies the lock pid via `ps` (no /proc — recycled pids read as "already running" forever). Multi-instance = one root/daemon per instance (`~/.vibespace/device@<dialhost>`), re-pair replaces within a root.** **REVERSE forward tcp-listen/tcp-accept/tcp-unlisten (2.148.0, the NAT-traversal tunnel)** — daemon binds 127.0.0.1:<port> ON THE DEVICE, accepts push back over the mux as new byte channels (chan ids from 0x40000000 — never collides with server-allocated 2..N; the tcp-accept control MUST precede channel data), server pipes them into its own loopback port; on link death the listener is DISOWNED not closed (port stays bound → reconnecting server re-owns same-port via connect-loop re-registration → remote mounts heal in place); both tcp paths backpressured (credit-after-drain + mux.onWritable resume); --stdio ssh bridge mode; --dial ws dial-out (Transport B; ws-min.js = hand-rolled RFC6455 client — the `head` bytes-with-the-101 upgrade trap is handled, dropping them ate first frames on fast reconnects)). client.js = DeviceManager (transports local/ssh, openSession/openPipeSession/fs*/runCmd/runStream/tcpForward/reverseForward/discovery). Server: /api/agentd-dial upgrade branch (dial-token gated, verifies hosts.dialTokenHash since 2.160.0) + dial-pair mint (writes the hash onto the dial host record; /api/agentd/devices + /api/device-mounts RETIRED in 2.160.0 — roster/test/unpair = /api/hosts, mounts = /api/machine-mounts, see machine-mounts.js). Pairing dialog has per-OS commands (mac/linux bash; WINDOWS EXPERIMENTAL via /agentd-install.ps1, PS 5.1-compatible + win32 named-pipe SOCK in the daemon). MULTI-INSTANCE pairing: dial-out installs root at ~/.vibespace/agentd@<dialhost> (per-instance daemon/tokens/bundle; installer exports VIBESPACE_AGENTD_ROOT — forget that and the daemon reads the default root's token). INSTALLER GOTCHA (2.152.1, real Mac report): macOS has NO setsid(1) — the installer's unconditional `setsid node …` started NOTHING and printed ✓ anyway (stderr redirected into agentd.out); now setsid-or-nohup + kill-0 verification before claiming success. E2E: scripts/dbg-pair-smoke.mjs (17 asserts, REAL daemon dial + mount chain + UI rows). Build: npm run build:agentd → data/bin/vibespace-agentd.js + vibespace-agentd-attach.js (both gitignored artifacts). Tests (all green, 3 environments incl AIDev real-ssh + fleet test pod): test-mux/-agentd/-agentd-session/-agentd-remote/-agentd-robustness (bidi/jitter/latency/concurrency)/-agentd-wired/-agentd-dial/-agentd-m3m4 (18 scenarios)/-agentd-switchover (real-host legacy-vs-device cross-checks). u-vstest soaks with ALL flags on.
  machine-mounts.js    — MachineMounts (B-f3e8 2.160.0 — HostMounts 2.147.0 + DeviceMounts 2.153.0 collapsed into ONE manager; records carry dir:'push'|'pull', keyed by hostId, store data/machine-mounts.json, both legacy stores constructor-migrated → .migrated; routes /api/machine-mounts* (POST :hostId {dir,…}), broadcast machine-mounts-updated). PUSH = mount THIS instance's folder ON the machine, OS-aware (Linux rclone/FUSE; macOS rclone/macFUSE else native mount_webdav — macFUSE probed ON the Mac since 2.160.0, the old check read the SERVER's /dev/fuse; Windows rclone/WinFsp else net use; rclone auto-installed remote-side w/ unzip→busybox→python3 fallbacks). Transport: _davBase prefers the agentd REVERSE-FORWARD TUNNEL (remote mounts http://127.0.0.1:<port>/dav over the device link — NAT-proof; dial machines tunnel-ONLY, ssh falls back to agentd.publicUrl); tunnelPort per record. PULL = the machine's folder mounted INTO this workspace over hosts.device(hostId) (serve-folder→tcp-forward→rclone webdav ro — works for ssh AND dial identically); live chain in-memory, restore()/onMachineLinked heal recorded pulls + re-own push tunnel ports (a re-dial means the daemon RE-EXECED → stale handles torn down first, real Mac report 2.158.1) + 90s child-process-ls health sweep (never node fs on a fuse mountpoint). unmount = best-effort remote teardown but ALWAYS token-revoke + record-drop (dead machine can't hold a credential); host removal → onMachineUnpaired drops all its mounts. GOTCHAS (real e2e catches): mint() returns {raw, rec} not {token,id}; NEVER execFileSync in anything sharing the process with /dav (event-loop block = FUSE IO hang); detached remote rclone needs FULL fd redirect (</dev/null >/dev/null 2>>log) or the ssh ControlMaster never frees; setsid is LINUX-ONLY — conditionally prefixed (macOS died at command-not-found with the error swallowed into the remote log, now tail'd back into the dialog); **TRAILING SLASH on a pull's shared path 403'd EVERY file (2.168.0, real walter Mac→VibeSpace report): the daemon serve-folder confines with `root + path.sep`, so a root ending in `/` (e.g. `/Users/me/Downloads/`) double-slashes the prefix (`…Downloads//`) — the root listing passes but every subpath 403s → rclone "couldn't list files: 403 Forbidden", mount never comes up. PUSH was immune (mountPush runs path.resolve). Fix strips the trailing slash in THREE places: mountPull (intake), _up (heals an existing record without a device-daemon update), serveFolder (daemon defense) — dbg-pair-smoke now pulls a trailing-slash path so its file-read assertion guards it.** Tests: test-machine-migrate.mjs (migration guard) + test-host-mounts(-tunnel).mjs (push e2e) + dbg-pair-smoke.mjs (pull e2e over a real dialed daemon)
  exit-proxy.js        — ExitProxyManager (task #164, 2.186.0): ON-DEMAND egress — an agent borrows a paired machine's network for a SINGLE command (a region / internal-VPN / fixed source IP), NOT the whole session. Two tiers via the `vibespace-exit` CLI (data/bin, static tracked, in AGENT_TOOLS): `use <machine>`/`url` = the device daemon serves a zero-dep in-daemon SOCKS5 (serve-socks/unserve-socks ops, CONNECT-only, DNS-on-exit) on its loopback, the server reaches it via the existing tcpForward and binds local `socks5h://127.0.0.1:<port>` (tool stays local, egress = the machine; proxy-aware TCP only); `run <machine> -- cmd` = execute natively on the machine via runCmd (universal fallback: ICMP/UDP/proxy-unaware/its DNS). Opt-in per machine (hosts.allowExit, default off — SSRF into its LAN; Remote-tab ↗ toggle). Routes: /api/exits + /api/hosts/:id/allow-exit (cookie UI) + /api/agent/exit[/use|/run] (vsst_). The loopback-only tunnel boundary holds (tcp-connect stays never-a-general-proxy; the SOCKS server is the one sanctioned egress, inside the machine owner's network).   port-forward.js      — PortForwardManager (B-0b60 tunnel path, 2.165.0): vscode-style port forwarding over the agentd data plane — NO frps/public exposure. detect(hostId) = `ss -tlnH || lsof -nP -iTCP -sTCP:LISTEN` over dm.runCmd (lsof matched FIRST — its `(LISTEN)` suffix;   plugins.js           — PluginManager (2.140.0, B-2d44): generic host-capability plugins — install + PERSISTENT state (~/.vibespace/plugins/<id>/, home=PVC in fleet) + boot replay (enabled+desiredUp → restart with server) + guided setup + status. Relay addr/port/token INJECTED via env `VIBESPACE_FRPS_ADDR/_PORT/_TOKEN` (fleet infra, NEVER in the repo — absent ⇒ `configured:false`, plugin no-ops). frpc runs with a base config + a local admin API (127.0.0.1:7400) + `includes` proxies dir; `frpPublish(name, localPort)` writes a per-port proxy toml, `frpc reload`s, polls the admin `/api/status` for `running` (retries a new public port in `VIBESPACE_FRP_PORT_MIN..MAX` on collision — the relay is fleet-shared), returns `http://<relay>:<port>/`. PortForwardManager.publish/unpublish wire it to a forward (persisted, re-published on restore). The relay itself (frps) is set up per the PRIVATE deploy dir runbook (39AI/vibespace-deploy/frp/), NOT this repo. **SUBDOMAIN mode + double-NAT pairing (2.183.0, B-5c1e): with `VIBESPACE_FRPS_SUBDOMAIN_HOST` set (or the plugin's subDomainHost config), frpPublish emits `type:https`+`https2http` proxies → `https://<sub>.<host>/` (persisted preferSub survives restarts). The Pair-a-device dialog's `viaRelay` option self-publishes the instance's own PORT and uses the relay subdomain as the dial base (bundle fetch + device-dial WS both route through it) — so a NAT'd instance can pair a NAT'd device (relay bridges both). Persisted selfDialSub keeps the URL stable across re-pairs. dial-pair route: `viaRelay` branch in server.js; plugin: setSelfDialSub/selfDialSub in status. PROTOCOL-AWARE publish (2.184.0): frpPublish `_probeProto`s the backend — HTTP→routed `type=http` subdomain (relay terminates TLS server-side w/ a wildcard cert via a Caddy front → browser-trusted, ZERO cert on instances), HTTPS→`https://ip:port` passthrough (backend's own cert), raw-TCP→`tcp://ip:port` (a DB/VNC has no Host/SNI). Never blindly https2http. `proto` rides the publish result + `publicProto` on the forward record. Relay side (private runbook): Caddy :443 wildcard-cert termination → frps vhostHTTP :8080; acme.sh Cloudflare DNS-01 auto-renew.** Test: scripts/test-frp-plugin.mjs (live, against the real relay)
  accounts.js          — AccountManager (per-session billing-identity switching, backend-scoped via a `backend` field on each account — legacy records = 'claude'. THREE account types: (1) Claude API key — AES-256-GCM in data/accounts.json + .accounts-key, injected as ANTHROPIC_API_KEY; (2) Claude SUBSCRIPTION (2.56.0) — a dir data/subs/<id>/ holding ONLY that account's .credentials.json, read by the CLI via CLAUDE_SECURESTORAGE_CONFIG_DIR (relocates the SECRET store ONLY; projects/sessions/settings stay in ~/.claude so transcripts+discovery stay shared — verified vs claude 2.1.205: Wde()=env??sn(). Empty dir→loggedIn:false, dir-with-creds→that login, ~/.claude untouched); (3) Codex/ChatGPT SUBSCRIPTION (2.59.0) — a dir data/codex-subs/cxs-<id>/ = an isolated CODEX_HOME whose sessions/+config.toml SYMLINK the shared ~/.codex (threads/settings shared, unified discovery — VERIFIED codex 0.142.5: symlinks survive a run, rollout lands in the shared dir), auth.json real per-account; createCodexSubscription/readCodexSubAuth(parses auth_mode + id_token JWT→email/plan)/finalizeCodexSubscription; login = `codex login --device-auth`. resolveForSpawn(requested, backend) returns {kind, localEnv:{VAR:val}, secret?, remoteCreds?} — claude-api→ANTHROPIC_API_KEY, claude-sub→CLAUDE_SECURESTORAGE_CONFIG_DIR, codex-sub→CODEX_HOME; all PROCESS-ENV only, never argv. Separate defaults per backend (defaultAccountId / defaultCodexAccountId). REMOTE (P3, 2.59.0): subscriptions ship their creds dir to a host via `remoteCreds` — ws-handler tars the whitelisted files (.credentials.json/.claude.json | auth.json), streams over ssh-stdin into 0700 ~/.vibespace/<subs|codex-subs>/<id>, symlinks shared subdirs, prefixes the env var; 2.59.1: NO rm -rf (concurrent same-account sessions), tar --keep-newer-files newest-wins (host-side refresh rotates the live token — don't clobber it) + poison-heal probe (remote creds file missing its validity marker is rm'd pre-extract). list() returns tail-8 for keys, email/plan/loggedIn for subs (read-only). importFromCli() captures a Console primaryApiKey. Lets the user's OWN subscription logins coexist per backend, switchable per session — the CLI's own /login only keeps one active at a time, so VibeSpace remembers each separately (like signing in/out without losing the others). **§ban-safety (2.59.1, after a real Max ban+refund — see [[reference_multi_subscription]]):** NO background /api/oauth/usage polling with sub tokens (that off-CLI fixed-cadence automated call on idle accounts is the #1 bot-flag: ToS §3.7 + 2026-02-20 OAuth-clarification) — usage is now captured PASSIVELY by data/bin/vibespace-usage (STATIC file), a statusLine hook injected via --settings into LOCAL TERMINAL sessions only that harvests the CLI's OWN rate_limits into data/usage-cache/<key>.json (zero API calls; chat/stream-json has no statusline → last-known; server ingestPassiveUsage reads the dir, no network). Subscription creds shipping to REMOTE is OFF by default (setting accounts.shipSubscriptionToRemote; ws-handler remoteAccountEnv gate throws with guidance) — a sub token from a datacenter IP is an impossible-travel/abuse signal; default = "log in on the host"; API keys always ship (sanctioned programmatic path))
  usage-history.js     — UsageHistory (2.61.0, codex 2.63.0): PERMANENT per-request token LEDGER for the Usage window. Mines Claude's OWN JSONL transcripts (terminal AND chat — mode-independent) AND Codex rollouts (~/.codex/sessions/**/rollout-*-<threadId>.jsonl: `event_msg`/`token_count` → `info.last_token_usage` = one request {input⊇cached, output⊇reasoning}; info:null = rate-limit heartbeat, skip; NO requestId → synthetic rid = `cx:<sid>:<cumulative total_tokens>` (strictly monotonic per thread — replays dedup); model/cwd from the preceding `turn_context` record PERSISTED IN THE CURSOR since incremental scans start mid-file; cw5/cw1 always 0 — rollouts don't report cache-write counts) into append-only monthly shards data/usage-history/events-YYYY-MM.ndjson; incremental per-file {offset,lastRid[,model,cwd]} byte cursor (offset is BYTES not string length — CJK bug, do not regress), reads CHUNKED via _scanFileLines (32MB slabs, complete-lines-only — a 1.9GB rollout exceeds Node's max string; first 2.3GB pass ≈8s, then incremental). **PERF (2.70.0):** /api/usage-stats used to re-read+re-parse EVERY shard per request — seconds of CPU at 218k events even on fast storage, and observed at 18s while a concurrent full-disk scan saturated IO (the workspace is a FUSE NFS mount; its IDLE baseline is fast — the '40ms/read' measured that day was contention, per the user's correction). Now: in-memory event cache (`_loadEvents` — shards are append-only, so after one full load each call reads only appended bytes, last-newline-aligned BYTE offsets; rid-dedup at load), scan() throttled 15s (force flag for the 3-min timer path), `_metaMap` TTL-cached 60s (66 tiny files = 2.7s over NFS), `_tier` memoized per model, `warm()` at boot (+8s). 18s→0.3s hot. DEDUP BY requestId TWICE (scan-time contiguous + read-time Set in _events — one request = 2-3 identical/sometimes-non-adjacent records). Account attribution BAKED per event (acct+atype: subscription/api/codex-subscription/global) PER-REQUEST-BY-TIME via attribution.ndjson (**2.84.0 ATTRIBUTION FIX, real data bug**: requests predating a session's FIRST attribution entry are GLOBAL (10-min grace for spawn skew) — the old `list[0].acct` fallback billed a week of pre-registration history to a newly added subscription during the initial 2.61.0 backfill (19.7k of Fish Max's 20.9k events were pre-registration); one-time `_maybeRebakeAttribution` (.attrib-rebake-v1 marker) rewrote 20,304 baked events) (appended from writeSessionMeta→recordUsageAttribution; sid = claudeSessionId||backendSessionId so codex threads attribute too) so sub $ and API $ NEVER mix. aggregate({from,to,backend,accounts}) → totals + series + groups(day/model/account/billing/project/mode/hour/weekday/session) (seq dims day/hour/weekday sort by KEY, not cost — cost-sorting scrambled the dashboard's hour axis, 2.180.2; the dashboard also self-sorts + gap-fills the closed hour/weekday scales + names weekdays); accounts = Set of bucket keys (account ids / '__global__' claude-global / '__global_codex__' codex-global — the two CLIs' machine logins are SEPARATE buckets since 2.64.0, billing keys 'cli-global-login'/'codex-cli-login') for the window's account filter. Pricing v2 pricing.json {tiers,accounts:{id:{discount}|{tiers}}} — account-aware _cost; _tier is DATA-DRIVEN (longest tiers-key substring match — new model = new pricing.json key, no code); official rates verified 2026-07-09 (Fable $10/$50, Opus 4.5-4.8 $5/$25, GPT-5.6 Sol $5/$30 Terra $2.5/$15 Luna $1/$6, GPT-5.5 $5/$30; missing default tiers back-fill into an existing pricing.json without clobbering edits). See [[project_usage_ledger]]
  session-status.js    — SessionStatusManager (session-level state/urgency set by the AGENT via vibespace-status CLI or by the user; user overrides of agent-set values record a pendingNotice injected as <system-reminder> into the NEXT chat-input; data/session-status.json — memory + session-status-updated broadcast are IMMEDIATE, disk write is DEBOUNCED 500ms + content-compared + flushed on exit (2.38.0), single-process so no race; independent of any task/context folder)
  user-todos.js        — UserTodoManager (2.65.0, the GLOBAL user-facing TODO list / "For you" inbox): discrete items an AGENT filed that need the USER (decision/input/review) — the inverse of the agent's own TodoWrite. One item = one owning session (sessionKey like session-status, webui:→backend rekey in the agent route); data/user-todos.json (session-status persistence pattern: debounced 500ms + content-compared + exit flush); add() idempotent BY TEXT across ALL statuses (open → refresh; resolved/dismissed → REOPEN the SAME id — review finding: fresh-id minting let an add→resolve loop or a dismissed-text re-file toast-spam every client despite the open cap); caps: 20 open/session (add throws with guidance), 1000 total (oldest RESOLVED pruned, open never); resolveByAgent by id or unique text substring (own session only); snapshot() = {open: urgency-then-newest sorted, resolved: last 15}; 'user-todos-updated' broadcast on every change. Client = src/lib/user-todos-panel.js. KNOWN LIMIT: webui:→backend rekey happens on the agent's NEXT call only (same as session-status) — in practice unreachable since vibespace-ask runs mid-turn when the backend id already exists. Client review fixes (do not regress): jump falls back to attachSession for a live session with NO open window (goToWindow is a no-op then); resync fetch on ws reconnect (items filed while offline stayed invisible); setStatus checks r.success (fetchJson never throws); knownIds includes the resolved tail (reopen must not self-toast). Panel detail+origin (2.69.1): item detail renders behind a collapsed `.ut-detail-exp` expander (open AND resolved rows — inline 2000-char details swamped the list); resolved rows carry the source session name (`.ut-sess`) and row-click jumps like open rows; clicks inside the expander are guarded from the row's jump-and-close

  webdav.js            — MountTokens (scoped bearer mount tokens, sha256-hashed, per-token chroot root + ro/rw) + registerWebdav (/dav WebDAV subset for VibeSpace↔VibeSpace mounting; auth = Bearer vsmt_ token, bypasses cookie auth, registered before json body parser)
  vnc.js               — VncManager (2.104.0, in-container desktop): LAZY lifecycle — POST /api/vnc/start spawns Xtigervnc (-localhost -SecurityTypes None, safe: the cookie-authed /api/vnc WS bridge is the ONLY route in) + XFCE session, both DETACHED (app restart keeps the desktop; boot ADOPTS an already-listening port — also the KasmVNC/bring-your-own path and the Xvfb+x11vnc test path). Env: VIBESPACE_VNC_PORT/DISPLAY/GEOMETRY. Client = src/lib/desktop-window.js ('desktop' window type, ⚙ menu entry gated on /api/vnc/status.available probed once at startup; noVNC is a SEPARATE ESM bundle public/novnc.js dynamic-imported on first use — top-level await can't live in the IIFE main bundle) **VNC BLACKLIST TRAP (2.111.1, real report 'Too many security failures'):** Xtigervnc launches with **`-UseBlacklist 0`** — MANDATORY, not optional. TigerVNC blacklists a source host after N unauthenticated connect-then-drop attempts (default 5, timeout doubles per strike); ALL desktop traffic is 127.0.0.1 (the bridge) AND `portListening()` connects+immediately destroys the socket on every status poll → TigerVNC counts each probe as a failure and locks localhost out. The cookie-authed bridge is the only route in, so the blacklist protects nothing. An already-tripped blacklist is in-memory: kill the stale Xtigervnc (or redeploy) to clear it.
  hosts.js             — HostManager (ssh host registry, connectivity test, keygen, remote discovery + first-user-message names, bootstrap, backend-status, dir-complete, fetchSessionJsonl = remote transcript → data/remote-jsonl cache; 2.129.0 remote-integration transparency: static AGENT_TOOLS list (ws-handler's per-spawn distribution reuses it), agentToolsStatus(id) = one read-only ssh round trip (per-tool sha256 — content compare, NOT mtime: hook/status are regenerated every local boot — + remote hook registration grep + node + keeper .sock count), installAgentTools (tar-over-stdin + hook-register), uninstallAgentTools (register --uninstall BEFORE rm; only our 6 files, .tok-* untouched). **`_hostShell(h, script)` (2.188.0) = the shared read-only probe channel: ssh hosts via _ssh, dial devices via dm.runCmd — backendStatus/accountsStatus/agentToolsStatus/cliPrimaryKey/readRemoteOAuth all route through it (they were ssh-only, so a selected dial device showed everything not-installed/unreachable; install/uninstall stay ssh-only — dial tools ship per-spawn). accountsStatus knows every claude auth shape (OAuth/primaryApiKey/apiKeyHelper — keep in sync with backendStatus's loginMethod chain, the 2.186.7/2.188.0 same-dialog-contradiction class) + returns host identity (claude config email; codex auth.json JWT email/plan decoded server-side). ⚠ CLI AUTH PRECEDENCE (2.191.0, verified by disassembling the 2.1.211 binary — CW-H200 incident): a configured `apiKeyHelper` in the MERGED settings UNCONDITIONALLY disables claude.ai OAuth (HS() gate), valid creds or not — so backendStatus/accountsStatus report `keyHelper` as an INDEPENDENT flag (never an elif rung) and Manage Agents warns "apiKeyHelper overrides this login" when both exist; the billing switcher explains why no pick can change it. `--settings '{"apiKeyHelper":null}'` is DROPPED by the CLI's field-level schema .catch (null fails string validation); `""` likely works but is unverified; forceLoginMethod only affects the login FLOW, not runtime precedence. 2.191.0 also: `fetchWorkflowState` (remote View Workflow — one compound probe, nonce-delimited payload, GNU-else-BSD stat, 2s TTL, ≤1MB for dial's runCmd stdout slice), `fetchAgentJsonl` + the generalized `_fetchRemoteByFind` core (fetchSessionJsonl's cache/invariants, parameterized find), and discovery sessions carry `pid` (Terminate on remote EXTERNAL cards reaches killRemotePid — it silently no-op'd without it).**)

  clerk-auth.js        — ClerkAuth (2.103.0, env-gated: VIBESPACE_CLERK_PUBLISHABLE_KEY = on-switch, frontend-API host + JWKS URL DERIVED from the key's base64 payload; VIBESPACE_CLERK_ALLOWED_EMAILS comma list, @domain = whole domain, EMPTY = reject all). verifyToken = pure node:crypto RS256 vs cached JWKS (1h TTL, unknown-kid rotation refetch, exp/nbf ±60s skew, iss check, alg pinned to RS256). REQUIRES an email claim in the token — Clerk dashboard: session-token custom claims {"email":"{{user.primary_email_address}}"} or a JWT template named 'vibespace' (login page tries template first).   agent-routes.js      — setupAgentRoutes() (2.93.0 split): every agent-facing endpoint — vibespace-ask/status/task routes, task-context/prompt-context injection (incl. user preamble + per-turn extras), stop-check nudge arbiter. Injection ORDER + SIZE are load-bearing — read the renderContext notes before touching payloads. TEACHING ARCHITECTURE (2.111.22-25, user-driven): the injected tools section is a DISCOVERY layer — per tool one trigger sentence + one fenced COPY-READY complete invocation (status sample carries --reason+--detail+--urgency; progress/ask carry --detail) so the first copied call is already valid; syntax/edge cases live in each CLI's own no-args output; hard rules enforce at point of use (waiting-state reason+detail rejection, success-output reminders). Don't grow the upfront block back into a rules dump (2.68.0 oversize incident is the other guardrail). **GROUP UPDATES DELIVER AS DIFFS (2.113.0, user request):** a mid-session group change no longer re-injects the whole group context — the session keeps a per-group SNAPSHOT of what it last saw (`s._groupSnap`, set at every delivery next to `_groupSeenAt`/`_ctxSig`; in-memory, restart ⇒ full re-delivery like the seen markers) and prompt-context injects a `<vibespace-task-update>` DELTA block (tasks.renderContextDiff: renamed / objective / backlog PARKED-RESOLVED-DROPPED-CLAIMED-UNCLAIMED-reworded-REMOVED one-liners (2.122.0; since 2.123.0 matched by the stable item id — occurrence-indexed text pairing retired — and TARGETED: `sessionKey` filters events to items the session created or claimed, everyone else keeps only the count pointer) / contextDir files updated-new-removed via old-vs-new `_ctxSig` / new activity entries LAST; ~5KB hard cap with tail-first truncation + `show --full` pointers; EMPTY diff = a no-op edit ⇒ nothing injected, markers still advance — the old code re-sent everything for those too; checklist deltas REMOVED with the feature in 2.121.0). No snapshot / setting `agents.contextUpdateDiffs` off ⇒ the old full "was UPDATED" payload. Also: FIRST-TIME groups on one prompt get ONE layered renderMultiContext (the codex first-prompt path) instead of N full payloads each repeating the ~2.3KB tools section — but ONLY when they cover the WHOLE membership (renderMultiContext states absolute membership; a subset call told a 3-group session "belongs to 2" — partial sets render per-group, count-free). REVIEW-HARDENED invariants (10-finding adversarial pass, do not regress; the checklist occurrence-indexed-diff one retired with the feature in 2.121.0): contextDir set/changed/cleared ⇒ diff returns null ⇒ FULL fallback (structural — the file index + folder conventions must be taught, a one-line path left pre-existing files invisible); the TASK.md pointer renders for LOCAL sessions only (remote ctx rsync excludes `.vibespace/`); contextDirSignature escapes `%`/`|` in paths (raw `|` sheared parse entries → wrong-path reports); **N CHANGED GROUPS COLLAPSE INTO ONE COMBINED BLOCK (2.113.1, user directive twice-clarified — 穿插/layered, the 2.68.0 class):** stacked per-group `<vibespace-task-update>` blocks + the ~2KB persisted-preview truncation could hide the very FACT that a 2nd group changed — `renderContextDiffMulti` (fed by `diffChanges`, which returns {lines, bits} where bits = phrase summaries like '3 new activity') renders ONE block whose HEADER line enumerates EVERY changed group + its summary, then per-group `##` sections SMALLEST-FIRST, 6.5KB cap with tail-first truncation (details die, the enumeration never does); ANY multi-block delivery (diff block + full re-deliveries + new-group fulls) is manifest-headed — `<vibespace-delivery-note>` naming EVERY block by group + the persisted-output rescue, diff block first, fulls last; combined parts >8KB with no rescue line get one prepended; markers/snapshot advance at RENDER, so a harness-dropped delivery (hook 3s timeout) stays lost until `show --full`/restart — ACCEPTED, same class as the seen-bump loss window. Tests: scripts/test-context-diff.mjs (store) + scripts/test-prompt-context.mjs (route, fake express)

top-6 + Other, labels from groups[splitBy] meta; Chart.js GOTCHA: every dataset MUST set yAxisID/xAxisID to the configured scale or a phantom default axis renders, Chart.js v4 (modular ~150KB, the ONLY chart lib since 2.98.0 — line/bar/doughnut all share one interaction model: formatted hover tooltips, legend series-toggling; bars auto-orient by dimension type; per-unit auto dual axes; instances MUST be destroyed via destroyCharts() before canvas removal — global registry + ResizeObserver leak otherwise; panels attach to the document BEFORE charts render or CSS-var color probes resolve black); 2.99.1: `.usage-body` is a container-type:inline-size container — `@container ≤700px` folds `.udash-grid` to 1 column so the layout tracks the WINDOW width (`.udash-add` spans `1 / -1`, NEVER `span 2` — in a 1-col grid `span 2` forces an implicit second track and the whole grid overflows); 2.99.2 h-scrollbar elimination invariants (verified 0 overflow 420–1100px, both views — do not regress): grid tracks `minmax(0,1fr)` never bare `1fr` (grid items default min-width:auto → one wide stat/table blows the track), `.udash-panel` is min-width:0 + its OWN container-type:inline-size (stat font `clamp(14px,10cqw,30px)` scales with the panel), `.udash-panel-body` overflow-x:auto contains table scroll, `.usage-seg` wraps, classic `.usage-grid` floors at `min(340px,100%)`, `.usage-body` overflow-x:hidden as the final guarantee; per-panel ✎ editor + ⋯ menu, presets, layout persisted in settings 'usage.dashboard'; pre-2.96 fixed layout = 'Classic view' escape hatch). Reads /api/usage-stats: headline tiles (est API-equivalent cost / total tokens = the 4 peer component tiles cached-read+cache-write+fresh-input+output / cache-hit-ratio / requests), daily-trend canvas bar chart, breakdowns by billing-type/account(type badges)/model/project/mode/cache-efficiency/hour/weekday/top-sessions, range filter (+ Custom… from/to date pickers, 2.63.0) + backend filter + ACCOUNT filter chips (2.63.0 — All/each account/CLI login; chip options UNION across loads so a narrow range doesn't drop chips; when app._usageGlobal.accountId links the CLI login to a named account the two render as ONE chip whose key is the comma pair), CSV export, + a built-in Pricing editor (tier list from pricing.tiers keys, per-account discount%, PATCH /api/usage-stats/pricing). Cost = estimate (subscriptions plan-covered). **DEVICE filter (2.128.0, user directive "hosts are devices, not accounts")**: a top-level 设备 row (All/This machine/each remote host) gates the WHOLE view via aggregate hostFilter (/api/usage-stats `host` param, matches ev.host||'local'); host buckets (type 'host') are EVICTED from the Account chips, and selecting a remote device hides the Account row entirely (remote usage = the host's own login) + clears any account filter. Remote data arrives via the 2.127.0 harvest (see data/bin/vibespace-usage-scan entry); harvest is CONSUMING (remote cursor advances) — tests must use VIBESPACE_USAGE_CURSOR temp paths, never production cursors (real incident: an e2e force-harvest ate the increment into a throwaway ledger and the UI looked unimplemented; rid-dedup made the cursor-reset re-harvest lossless)
  sidebar-render-mobile.js — Mobile sidebar mixin (two-level folder/group navigation)
    mobile-nav.js      — MobileNav class (window switcher, close, desktop tabs, gestures; 2.99.0: ⚙ gear → gs-menu + worst-of quota donut chip → usage popup — the taskbar with ALL its entry points is hidden ≤768px, these are the phone's ONLY paths to Usage/Manage-agents/Diagnostics/quota/account-switching; chip rendered by usage-meter's _renderUsage with its own change-guard, popup+gs-popover clamp to full-width sheets via stylesheet !important beating the JS anchor's inline position)

    stage-manager.js   — StageManager (2.112.0 dynamic desktop 'Stage', default OFF via desktop.dynamicEnabled — docs/design-dynamic-desktop.md is the blueprint+progress anchor. VIEW model: one window two geometries (home gridBounds vs shared slot); materialization intercepts wm.focusWindow (_stageBypass prevents recursion; createWindow's tail focus flows through it too); per-hero aux workspaces = {openSpec, stageBounds, extras(scroll walker)} in SyncStore 'stage' (slot/ws:<key>/lru), heroKey RE-DERIVED AT RECORD TIME (backendSessionId arrives late); placeholder is a REAL wm window type 'stage-placeholder' — onWindowCreated MUST check the TYPE, the _isStagePlaceholder flag lands after createWindow's tail hook (smoke-caught: placeholder got swept as transient); incoming hero z-stacks at BOTTOM (moved slot must not cover a recorded workspace); LRU evicts hidden AUX only — session windows are NEVER closed by the stage (walter's killed-session lesson); desktop autosave is SUPPRESSED while staged (layout.js gate) — stage state never leaks into desktop records; walter's four defenses ported: serialized latest-wins switches, keyed replay dedup 15s, programmatic-switch guard, separate _hiddenByStage flag. RESTORATION MATRIX (2.112.1-2, design §4b, all 17 openSpec actions): durable=file/info-probed then replayed; derived=archive-entry temps carry via:{archive,entry} recipe and RE-EXTRACT on replay (the zip-PDF case); volatile=blob/data pages+recipe-less temps+DIRTY EDITORS (winInfo._editorDirty(), CodeEditor.modified exposed 2.112.2) are NEVER LRU-evicted and skip+one-toast when dead at replay; deleted task groups + 404 workflows pre-checked. INIT-ORDER GOTCHA (2.112.3, real 'placeholder never moves' report): stage.init() MUST run after initStateSync — StateSync.set() SILENTLY DROPS writes for unregistered stores, so the slot never persisted while dragging worked fine; _sync() lazily registers the store on any access as the guard. Any new SyncStore consumer needs the same care. **2.112.4 field fixes (4 user reports, CDP-smoke-verified — do not regress):** ① leave()/_deactivateHero HAND THE HERO BACK to the desktop system — restore _stageHomeBounds→gridBounds, clear _isStageHero/_onStage (off-stage moves edit HOME bounds, not the slot), then dm._hideWin/target-show like a normal desktop window (bare _hideStage left it invisible on its home desktop AND at slot size — the reported bug); enter() re-borrows via the still-set _heroWinId with a FRESH home snapshot; STAGE_ID-created heroes have no home and stay stage-hidden; _materializeInner clears stale _hiddenByDesktop. ② stage grid persists via stage-store key 'grid' — the interception lives at the TOP of scheduleAutoSave (NOT _doAutoSave: the _restoring gates dropped the call before the stage gate ran, smoke-caught); enter() applies it. ③ stage↔desktop window drags blocked BOTH directions (user directive superseding the design-§4 unbind+move): stage.dragToDesktopBlocked(win) gates window.js preview hover + dm.moveWindowToDesktop (covers the right-click menu too); placeholder additionally healStray()-recaptured + excluded from captureState (real report: escaped placeholder stuck on a desktop). ④ desktop.dynamicEnabled applies LIVE (init() settings listener → render kick / leave-if-disabled); same class fixed in sidebar for sessionCard.* card-build-time settings — a liveApply:true schema flag is a CLAIM, every render-time-read setting needs a change listener that re-renders its surface. **2.112.5 MULTI-CLIENT (real cross-client window-loss report — do not regress):** materializing a session with NO local window used to mint a stage-owned hero under a FRESH winId; leaving to the desktop holding that session per OTHER clients' records captured a state missing the recorded winId → the broadcast CLOSED the window on every client. Fix = IDENTITY ADOPTION: `_adoptDesktopIdentity` scans dm._savedStates for the session and converges (wm.rekeyWindow onto the recorded winId — chain-less windows only — + home desktop/gridBounds/isMaximized), retried at leave/_deactivateHero for late ids (resume fills openSpec async). Structural gotchas: createWindow's TAIL focus runs materialization BEFORE app.js's desktop-tag wrapper assigns _desktopId (adoption gate accepts !win._desktopId; the wrapper must not clobber an id set during creation); maximized heroes un-maximize onto the slot and hand-back applies home element geometry BEFORE re-maximizing (toggleMaximize must record HOME px as prevBounds). Live sync: init() subscribes 'stage'/'*' (StateSync fires for REMOTE ops only) — slot → re-apply to occupant, grid → setGrid, ws:<activeHeroKey> → debounced _reconcileWorkspace (restore + close-absent aux, dirty editors exempt); _scheduleRecord(500ms) on aux create/move keeps records live. **Hero is SHARED across clients (2.112.6, user directive — 挂机/walk-over): 'hero' store key {key, openSpec}; _publishHero at materialize (skip while _applyingRemoteHero), _followRemoteHero on remote ops (pointer-down deferred) + at enter (shared hero WINS over the tab's stale hero); hero close → clear → placeholder everywhere; only staged-or-not stays per-tab. closeWindow auto-focus-next (and applyLayout/overlap filters) must skip _hiddenByStage — a stage-hidden previous hero got auto-focused on hero close and re-materialized fleet-wide (harness-caught).** **2.151.0 preview fixes (2nd ghost report — do not regress):** ① the 2.134.0 home-bounds substitution in dm._renderSwitcher read `_stageHomeBounds?.gridBounds` but _stageHomeBounds IS the flat bounds object → always undefined → hero ghost-painted at the SLOT position on its home preview for 17 releases (shape-mismatch no-op; now reads the flat shape); ② the preview render DIGEST must cover every field the render filters on — _hiddenByDesktop/_hiddenByStage/_onStage were missing, so leave()'s intermediate setGrid-triggered render (target windows still hidden) cached a BLANK preview and the post-show render early-returned (preview stayed white until visiting another desktop); leave() also mirrors switchTo's +400/+1300ms refreshSwitcher retries. COMMITTED smoke: scripts/test-stage-preview.mjs (throwaway git-worktree server + headless-chrome raw CDP, 9 assertions through the REAL materialize/leave paths — replaces the ephemeral harnesses). Verified: 2-CDP-client harness 10/10 + single-client 11/11 — harness needs --disable-background-timer-throttling + real per-client input for _userDirty. **2.209.0 pile-at-slot rootfix (walter's 超级重叠 — Stage↔desktop round trip stacked every stage-born session at the slot, accumulating per trip; repro'd 16/16 then fixed, scripts/test-stage-overlap.mjs): ① enter() re-shows ONLY the live workspace (remembered hero + aux bound to _heroKey/'__pending__') — the blanket every-_hiddenByStage re-show resurrected every slot-PARKED ex-hero; ② _borrowHero ALWAYS creates a home snapshot BEFORE applying the slot (a window born while staged has no gridBounds at the synchronous creation-tail borrow → pixel _captureGridBounds first — safe, stage flags not yet set — else _cascadeHome(); slot-near bounds never become home) and _handBackHero has a cascade belt for pre-fix degenerated field state — without this the slot was the window's ONLY geometry forever; ③ dm.switchTo routes through stage.leave()/enter() while staged and treats '__stage__' as never-a-target — a raw switchTo (add-desktop +, command-mode d/D, moveSessionWindow, _onRemoteDesktopUpdated) captured the stage's window set under desktops['__stage__'] (lazy-replayed later as REAL windows at slot bounds) and left stage._active desynced; client boot + server layout-sync both refuse-and-scrub the poisoned record; ④ _onRemoteDesktopUpdated exempts STAGE_ID windows from deleted-desktop reassignment (any remote desktop meta change used to retag the whole stage onto a normal desktop) and never force-switches a staged client; ⑤ _materializeInner aborts when !_active (queued materialize firing post-leave); ⑥ leave() validates the target desktop still exists (remote-deleted _prevDesktopId). KNOWN MINOR (parked): stale shared-hero follow — _publishHero early-returns on null _heroKey with no retry at id adoption, so multi-client walk-over can follow an outdated hero record.**
    external-editor.js — Ctrl+G split-pane CodeMirror editor (extracted from app.js)
```

## Developer Guide: Where to Find & Modify Code

### Common Tasks → File Location Map

| Task | Primary File(s) | Notes |
|------|-----------------|-------|
| **Add/change terminal behavior** | `src/lib/terminal.js` | xterm.js config, input filtering, cursor, font |
| **Session list / sidebar** | `src/lib/sidebar.js` + `src/lib/sidebar-state.js` + `src/lib/sidebar-render.js` + `src/lib/sidebar-render-mobile.js` + `src/lib/sidebar-workbench.js` (Folders tab) + `src/lib/sidebar-mounts.js` (Remote tab) + `src/lib/session-card.js` | Sidebar shell + state mixin + render mixin (desktop) + render mixin (mobile) + Folders-tab workbench + Remote-tab mounts + card factory |
| **Backend metadata / icons** | `src/lib/agent-meta.js` | Backend/agent meta, createBackendIcon, createModeBackendIcon, contrast adaptation |
| **Session discovery (RUNNING/STOPPED)** | `src/routes/sessions.js` + `src/session-store.js` | Lock-first algorithm, tmux detection, PID verification |
| **Window tiling / grid / snap** | `src/lib/window.js` | Drag, resize, grid cells, layout presets, freeform, Alt bypass, overlap switcher, pre-snap size memory, move mode |
| **Tab groups** | `src/lib/tab-group.js` | Drag icon-to-icon to merge windows into tabs, Chrome-style tab bar, drag-out to split |
| **Custom grid presets** | `src/lib/app.js` → `_addCustomGrid()` + `src/routes/persistence.js` | + button adds, right-click removes, persisted in layouts.json |
| **Session starring** | `src/lib/sidebar.js` → `toggleStar()`, `isStarred()` | ★/☆ per session, starred first in sidebar + taskbar |
| **Task system / board** | `src/task-groups.js` + `src/lib/sidebar-tasks.js` + `src/lib/task-detail.js` | tasks.json store, board (Tasks tab), bind-as-tag, detail window, attention — design in docs/design-task-system.md |
| **Workflow detail viewer** | `src/lib/workflow-detail.js` + `src/routes/sessions.js` (`/api/workflow`) + `chat-renderers.js` (View Workflow btn) | Post-hoc dynamic-workflow/ultracode viewer; reads terminal `wf_<runId>.json` snapshot; per-agent View Log reuses subagent viewer |
| **Session rename** | `src/lib/sidebar.js` → `renameSession()` | Double-click name in sidebar, syncs to open windows via `app.syncSessionName()` |
| **Ctrl+G external editor** | `server.js` → `createEditorHelper()` + `src/lib/external-editor.js` | Fake "code" script + split-pane CodeMirror |
| **File viewer (open file)** | `src/lib/file-viewer.js` | Dispatch by type, size check, binary detection |
| **Code editor** | `src/lib/code-editor.js` | CodeMirror 6, language switching, Prettier/server-side format, markdown/HTML preview |
| **Chat mode** | `src/lib/chat-view.js` (controller) + `src/lib/chat-renderers.js` (rendering) | Virtual scroll, op dispatch, message rendering, tool cards |
| **Chat input / send** | `src/lib/chat-input.js` | Textarea, attachments, slash commands, draft persistence, TODO display |
| **Chat status bar** | `src/lib/chat-status-bar.js` | Model, context%, cost, permission mode dropdown, task popup |
| **Chat search** | `src/lib/chat-search.js` | Ctrl+F, CSS Custom Highlight API, server-side search |
| **Chat minimap** | `src/lib/chat-minimap.js` | Semantic scrollbar, turn markers, drag-to-jump |
| **Hex viewer** | `src/lib/hex-viewer.js` | Binary display with chunked loading |
| **Themes / colors** | `src/lib/themes.js` + `public/style.css` | 6 built-in themes, CSS variables `[data-theme="..."]` |
| **Theme editor** | `src/lib/theme-editor.js` + `public/theme-editor.css` | Floating panel: ~50 CSS vars + 16 ANSI, live preview, save/load/delete |
| **Layout save/restore + sync** | `src/lib/layout.js` + `src/ws-handler.js` | Auto-save debounce, layout-sync WS protocol, openSpec pattern |
| **Virtual desktops** | `src/lib/desktop-manager.js` + `src/ws-handler.js` | Create/delete/rename/switch desktops, Ubuntu-style previews, per-desktop grid, drag-to-move, multi-client sync |
| **Usage / rate limits** | `server.js` → `refreshRateLimit()` + `src/lib/app.js` → `_pollUsage()` | Non-billable `GET /api/oauth/usage` poll (read-only token, 429 backoff), every ~5 min (the billable Haiku approach was superseded 2026-06-22 — see §9) |
| **WebSocket protocol** | `src/ws-handler.js` + `src/lib/ws.js` | All WS message types in ws-handler switch/case |
| **State sync / drafts** | `src/sync-store.js` + `src/lib/utils.js` → `StateSync` class | Versioned diff broadcast, reconnect recovery, draft persistence |
| **Syntax highlighting** | `src/lib/highlight.js` + `src/lib/chat-renderers.js` | 30 hljs languages, line numbers, language picker |

| **Taskbar** | `src/lib/taskbar.js` | Taskbar rendering, window list popup, right-click context menu |
| **Command mode** | `src/lib/command-mode.js` | Ctrl+\ prefix key, tmux-style window commands |
| **Embedded browser** | `src/lib/browser-window.js` | iframe + URL bar + proxy toggle |
| **Shared utilities** | `src/lib/utils.js` | escHtml, createPopover, showContextMenu, fetchJson, copyText, StateSync |
