- Desktop switch `display:none` broke chat scroll: `display:none` collapses layout, losing scroll position. Fix: use `visibility:hidden` + `pointer-events:none` instead — preserves all internal state.
- Desktop delete lost hidden windows: non-active desktop windows stayed `visibility:hidden` after reassignment. Fix: show new active desktop's windows before reassigning deleted desktop's windows. Unloaded windows (never visited) restored via `layoutManager.restoreState()`.
- Desktop drag same-desktop drop: mini rect position wasn't applied — window disappeared. Fix: apply mini rect as `gridBounds` + `_applyGridBounds()` for same-desktop drops.
- Layout presets affected other desktops: `applyLayout` iterated all windows. Fix: filter by `_desktopId === activeDesktop` and `!_hiddenByDesktop`.
- Desktop preview empty after refresh: non-active desktops had no live windows. Fix: fall back to `_savedStates` cached data.
- Usage pie border artifact: `border` on `conic-gradient` circle caused bright seams. Fix: replaced with `box-shadow: 0 0 0 1px`.
- Active count always 0: filtered `type==='terminal'` only. Fix: count all windows on active desktop, renamed to "N windows".
- Duplicate sessions on macOS: same JSONL in multiple project dirs (CJK path encoding). Fix: `sessionMap` deduplicates by sessionId, running status wins over stopped.
- Usage not showing on macOS: credentials stored in Keychain not `.credentials.json`. Fix: `security find-generic-password -s "Claude Code-credentials" -a <user> -w` fallback.
- Settings search filter persisted after close/reopen: `_search` not cleared on `_showDialog()`. Fix: reset to `''` on open.
- Permission state lost across refresh/restart: `control_response` not in buffer, `control_request` stripped from raw(), `_processResult` flushed pending permission tools. Fix: record responses in buffer, pass control messages to normalizer, search backwards for flushed tools, auto-resolve completed tools.
- Composite icon invisible on dark themes: `opacity:0.15` fill, wrong `currentColor` inheritance, missing `data-backend` for contrast system. Fix: mode badge approach with `var(--text)` SVG + backend logo mask.
- Duplicate sessions on macOS: same JSONL in multiple project dirs (CJK path encoding). Fix: `sessionMap` deduplicates by sessionId, running status wins over stopped.
- Usage not showing on macOS: credentials stored in Keychain not `.credentials.json`. Fix: `security find-generic-password -s "Claude Code-credentials" -a <user> -w` fallback.
- macOS auto-update build failure: non-login shells lack Homebrew PATH. Fix: prepend `path.dirname(process.execPath)` to child process env.
- Tab merge targeting wrong window: Map iteration order != z-index. Fix: compare all matches by z-index, pick highest.
- Settings text inputs unstyled in dark themes: `.settings-input-text` had no CSS rule. Fix: added themed rule matching other settings controls.
- Settings multi-select layout broken: multi-select controls squeezed label. Fix: `:has(.settings-multi-select)` wraps control to full width below label.
- Interrupt killing session instead of stopping turn: Claude Code newer versions exit on SIGINT. `postInterrupt` always sent SIGINT as a "dual-interrupt" safety net (for bugs #17466, #3455), but in recent versions this kills the whole session and leaves chat read-only. Fix: delay SIGINT by 2s, re-read wrapper meta before firing; if `streaming:false` skip. Sending a new chat message cancels the pending SIGINT.
- Read-only chat windows had no way to continue: user had to close window and resume from sidebar. Fix: all read-only ChatViews (view-history, terminate, exit) show "Resume this session" button in place of input area; click calls `app.resumeSession()` + closes the read-only window. Subagent viewers skip.
- Tab merge hit-test matched occluded icons: dragging A's titlebar onto A's own position would merge with a stacked window B underneath (because `getBoundingClientRect` ignores occlusion). Fix: use `elementFromPoint` after temporarily disabling `pointer-events` on the dragged element; match the `.window` ancestor. Extracted into shared `_detectTabMergeTarget` helper on tab-group mixin, used by all three drag paths (titleBar, icon drag, tab drag-out). Side benefit: window.js was checking for `.tab-bar` (wrong class name — actual is `.tab-bar-tabs`), so tab-bar merge drops never worked; now they do.
- Tab drag-out couldn't merge: `_setupTabDrag`'s onMove only ran snap detection. Fix: also run the merge hit-test and on drop call `addToTabChain`/`createTabChain`.
- Tab drag-out preview confusing over merge zones: the detached window IS the cursor-following preview (no separate ghost), but while hovering a tab zone it was being hidden — users saw nothing. Fix: mirror the titleBar drag pattern exactly — window follows cursor normally in empty space; on entering merge zone, window `display:none` and a small `.tab-ghost` preview appears; on leaving, restore window and resume cursor tracking.
- Icon drag didn't hide source: the dragging icon's source window stayed visible while the ghost followed the cursor. Fix: `visibility:hidden` source on drag threshold crossed, restored on mouseup.
- Tab drag-out window drifted behind others: `_detachFromChain` copied the host's z-index, so the detached window might end up below a focused standalone window. Fix: call `focusWindow(winId)` right after detach.
- HTML preview broken for pages with relative resources: `srcdoc` has no base URL, and `sandbox='allow-scripts'` blocked same-origin loading. Fix: inject `<base href="/api/file/serve/DIR/">` into srcdoc, add `allow-same-origin` to sandbox. New path-based route `GET /api/file/serve/*` maps URL path segments to filesystem paths for proper `<base href>` resolution.
- HTML preview didn't re-render on resize: JS-computed layouts (canvas, calculated dimensions) froze at initial window size. Fix: ResizeObserver on preview body triggers debounced (300ms) srcdoc rewrite.
- Upload progress bar fill invisible: `<span>` fill element was `display:inline`, CSS width/height had no effect. Fix: `display:block`.
- Upload popover had no background: missing `background/border/box-shadow` CSS on `.upload-popover`.
- Popovers/context menus clipped by viewport edge: no bounds checking after render. Fix: `createPopover` uses rAF + `getBoundingClientRect` to clamp all four edges; `showContextMenu` clamps synchronously after items appended. Both render with `visibility:hidden` first then reveal.
- Model discovery failed for OAuth users: `/v1/models` returned 401 for OAuth tokens → switched to `/api/claude_cli/bootstrap`. Later (~2026-06) bootstrap's `additional_model_options` went null AND `/v1/models` started accepting OAuth Bearer → switched back to `/v1/models` for both auth types (new fable tier was missing until then).
- OAuth token expired silently: server cached only the accessToken with no refresh. Fix: store full creds (accessToken + refreshToken + expiresAt), auto-refresh via `platform.claude.com/v1/oauth/token` when expired. `getOAuthToken(callback)` async API with refresh, sync fallback for non-critical paths.
- Resume/new session fails on older Claude CLI (`--name` unsupported): Claude Code <2.1.98 doesn't have `--name`, causing `error: unknown option` → exit code 1 → immediate read-only. Fix: parse `claude --help` at startup for `--name` support (`CLAUDE_SUPPORTS_NAME`), propagate to adapter config. `buildSessionArgs` only includes `--name` when supported.
- Dead sessions lost on server restart: layout restore silently dropped windows when dtach processes died. Fix: fallback to `viewSession()` (read-only JSONL history + Resume button). `captureState` now saves `cwd`, `restoreState` fetches `/api/sessions` for stopped session lookup.
- Broken pty stdin false positive: auto-detect killed working pty when API was slow. Buffer-growth check still failed for opus[1m] (10-30s before first token). Fix: wrapper writes `_stdin_ack` to stdout immediately on receiving stdin input; server checks for this ack instead of buffer growth. Immune to model latency.
- Codex thinking messages lost during/after tool calls: `_finalizeStreaming()` cleared reasoning map prematurely; `_processReasoningItem()` created duplicates. Fix: only finalize reasoning on turn-end; finalized items update existing streaming messages in-place.
- Lazy folder rendering: IntersectionObserver ignored `'pending'` state for off-screen folders. Fix: handle both `'pending'` and `'placeholder'`.
- Thinking/streaming state not syncing across clients: attach response `isStreaming` only read wrapper meta (can lag due to debounced writes). Fix: also check normalizer messages for `status==='streaming'`. `_reattach()` now calls `_syncTypingIndicator()` after catch-up.
- Stale streaming messages causing permanent 'responding' indicator: `_finalizeStreaming()` broke at first non-streaming message, leaving interleaved stale ones. Fix: scan to `role==='user'` boundary. `_deriveTypingLabel` also stops at user messages to ignore stale turns. `isStreaming` in attach response used `||` (stale meta overrode normalizer); fixed to prefer normalizer when it has messages.
- Broken pty stdin false positives with old wrappers: new server expected `_stdin_ack` but old running wrappers didn't send it. Fix: fallback to buffer growth check when no ack received.
- `/compact` leaving chat stuck on 'thinking': stream-json emits `user` messages (compact summary) but no `result` after `/compact`. `_processUser` never called `_finalizeStreaming`, so stale streaming assistant messages persisted indefinitely. Fix: `_processUser` now calls `_finalizeStreaming` at start of new user message. Wrapper also treats `compact_boundary` system message as end-of-stream (`meta.streaming = false`).
- Codex resume lost old history: `thread/resume` always creates a new thread ID (fork by design). Server overwrote `backendSessionId` with new ID, losing the old one. Fix: track `forkedFrom` array (chain of old thread IDs). `CodexSessionMessages._ensureParsed` loads the full chain (oldest → newest) + current, merging with fingerprint dedup. Forked-from threads hidden from sidebar to avoid duplicates. Persisted in session metadata, survives server restarts. Supports multi-level forks (A → B → C).
- Model switch stuck on 'thinking...': the `set_model` confirmation echo (`<local-command-stdout>Set model to ...`) is a user record with NO turn behind it — the streaming tracker (server turn-lifecycle block + chat-wrapper meta.streaming) treated every user record as a turn start and waited forever for a result. Both now skip user records whose text starts with `<local-command-` (any local command echo).
- isStreaming derived from stale normalizer messages: old heuristic scanned normalizer messages for `status==='streaming'`, but `processLive` could create streaming entries before `convertHistory` finalized them (race on server restart). Fix: replaced with explicit `session._isStreaming` flag tracked from protocol signals (Claude: `result`/`compact_boundary`/`user`; Codex: `task_started`/`task_complete`/`turn_aborted`/`task_failed`). Also set immediately on `chat-input` send (no round-trip delay). Initialized from wrapper metadata on restore, cleared on exit. Single source of truth — no more heuristic.
- Session history lost after server restart: attach only loaded JSONL when `normalizer.total === 0`, but PTY `processLive` could populate partial buffer data first, so the full JSONL history (e.g. 4367 messages) was skipped (only 63 buffer messages shown). Fix: `_historyLoaded` flag; on first attach, re-create the normalizer and `convertHistory(sm.raw())` from full JSONL + buffer regardless of `processLive` having added partial data.
- Duplicate Codex messages from JSONL/buffer overlap: JSONL records carry `item_id` that buffer records lack, so `JSON.stringify(payload)` fingerprints differed and `mergeCodexRecords` dedup failed. Fix: strip `item_id`/`itemId` before fingerprinting `response_item`/`event_msg` records.
- Terminated (read-only) windows lost their identity (2.71.0, two user reports): the server session vanishes from the live list on kill (discovery re-lists it STOPPED with no webuiId), so (a) the Resume bar's `_getSessionIds` found nothing and `_resumeAndClose` silently no-op'd, and (b) `_notifySidebarFocus` cleared the sidebar highlight instead of highlighting the stopped card. Both now fall back to the identity captured in `winInfo._openSpec` (backend/backendSessionId/cwd, kept fresh by syncSessionIdentity while live) — the highlight fallback also covers view-history windows.
- Resume opening a second window for a terminated conversation: clicking sidebar Resume while a terminated (read-only) window for the same session was still open created a duplicate stuck window. Fix: `resumeSession` closes any window whose `_openSpec.backendSessionId` matches the target before creating the resumed window.
- File explorer Copy Path no-op over HTTP: `navigator.clipboard` is undefined in non-HTTPS contexts, so `navigator.clipboard?.writeText(...)` short-circuited to `undefined` and the `.catch` fallback never ran. Fix: use shared `copyText()` utility (handles the `execCommand` fallback).
- AskUserQuestion unanswerable in chat: rendered as a generic tool card with raw JSON. Fix: normalizer marks `permission.kind='user_input'` + `questions`; renderer shows interactive paginated questionnaire; response uses `approved:true` + `toolInput.answers` keyed by question text.
- `/goal` not working in stream-json mode (CLI ≤2.1.139): slash commands were terminal-only, so the wrapper simulated auto-continue after `result`. SUPERSEDED 2026-06-09: CLI ~2.1.1xx added `supportsNonInteractive` to `/goal` — the wrapper now forwards the native command, the Stop hook drives continuation/met-detection, and the server tails the JSONL for `goal_status` attachments (JSONL-only, not on stdout). Codex was native from the start (`thread/goal/set` RPC).
- Codex goal state wrong/zero on attach: tried to reconstruct from JSONL scan (format changed across versions: `<untrusted_objective>`→`<objective>`, `role:developer`→`role:user`) and wrapper meta with race conditions. Fix: query `thread/goal/get` (authoritative; camelCase `timeUsedSeconds`/`tokensUsed`) on startup + after each turn; wrapper meta is single source of truth; read goal fields in `restoreSessions` (not just attach, since `_goal` set during restore skipped the re-read).
- Codex `apply_patch` Update cards expanded by default: `renderPatchDiff` had `open` on the diff `<details>`. Fix: removed `open` to collapse like other tool cards.
- Huge sessions (>512MB JSONL) — tail-only load + continuous seek scroll (no seam marker): `readFileSync(fp,'utf-8')` THROWS past Node's ~512MB max string length (swallowed error → blank chat). `readJsonlBounded` (codex adapter, shared with Claude session-store) with `{tailOnly:true}` loads a line-aligned last-32MB TAIL only — NO head, NO elision seam marker (the old head+2MB+seam+tail model is gone). The whole earlier history is one continuous virtual scroll: `ChatView._installSeekSentinel` puts an invisible 1px `.chat-gap-sentinel` at the top of the tail; an IntersectionObserver + scroll-driven `_maybeSeekEarlier` call `_loadEarlierGap`, which seek-reads one ~2000-record slab older each time (`/api/session-history-gap?endLine=N&count=C`), walking the cursor from `tailStartLine` down to line 0 (`_finishSeek` removes the sentinel at 0). Gap messages carry `.chat-gap-msg`, are excluded from virtual-scroll trim + `_windowStart/_windowEnd` accounting, render read-only (orphan tool results where the call is outside the slab — acceptable). Seek primitives: `getJsonlLineIndex` caches a line→byte-offset table (streaming Buffer scan, no >512MB string; EXTENDS incrementally — append-only growth scans only the new tail bytes, so seeks stay ~15ms even while a live session keeps writing, instead of re-streaming 100s of MB per jump); `jsonlGapInfo` gives `{tailStartLine, totalLines}`; `readJsonlLineRange` seek-reads any raw line range (records tagged `__line`). `?info=1` returns the gap; `?endLine`/`?startLine=N&count=C` seek-normalize a slab (subagent-filtered to match the display path); `&whole=1` unclamps the read to `[0,totalLines)` (default clamps to `[0,tailStartLine)` so continuous scroll-up never re-reads the registered tail). JUMPS (search + minimap) TELEPORT by ABSOLUTE FILE LINE — immune to normalized-index drift AND to the live tail sliding forward as the file grows. `ChatView._seekTeleport(line)` replaces the whole view with a `whole=1` slab centered on the line (±300 lines), keeps+resets the sentinel (scroll-up continues by line), sets `_teleported` + `_gapCursorDown`, and shows the scroll-to-bottom button as 'return to latest' (click → `jumpToBottom` restores the live registered tail, `_resetGapAfterJump` clears `_teleported`). Teleport browsing is BIDIRECTIONAL: scrolling down seek-loads newer slabs (`_maybeSeekLater`/`_loadLaterGap`, cursor `_gapCursorDown`, 3s idle backoff at file end) and the DOM is capped by `_trimGapDom(side, cap=3400, keep=2400)` which drops far-side elements and REWINDS the corresponding cursor so scrolling back re-loads them — the cap MUST exceed teleport slab + one full 2000-line slab (~1200 msgs) per direction or up/down loads thrash each other's content. content-visibility is force-disabled only while the jump LANDS (stable heights → sync scroll hits), then `_setStableHeights(false)` re-enables it ~1.6s later. The collapse of never-cv-rendered elements is ASYNC (relevancy decided at paint) — scrollHeight shrinks hugely + scrollTop clamps, so scroll-delta compensation FIGHTS native scroll anchoring (observed scrollTop yanked to 0; view relocated ~1.5s after landing). Correct approach: on restore, REPLAY the landing — `_scrollElStable(this._lastJumpTargetEl)` or the search's recorded `_lastRevealRun` (exact range inside a tall message), skipped if the user scrolled since the jump (`_lastUserScrollAt`). A match already RENDERED in the live view (|element ts − match ts| < 2s) scrolls directly — no teleport (replacing the live view for something on screen was jarring); same fast path in `_jumpToFileTime` via `_scrollToNearestTs(ts, 2000)`. The pos indicator hides while teleported (its window-index numbers are stale). The `.chat-search-flash` overlay parents inside the chat container (absolute, host-relative coords) NOT document.body — a body-level fixed overlay draws over other windows stacked above. One jump primitive: `jumpToFileMatch` (search) and `_jumpToFileTime` (minimap) both teleport, so there is NO index-drift path left. Landing is content-visibility-proof: `_scrollElStable` / ChatSearch `_revealNearest` re-center over ~12 rAF frames + timed re-centers at 180/400/750ms (heights keep computing for ~1s after a big slab loads); `_revealNearest`/`_revealInEl` route through `_scrollToRange`, which handles FOUR reveal blockers: (a) most tool cards are COLLAPSED `<details>` — `_expandRangeAncestors` opens the match's whole ancestor chain first (+ forces content-visibility on the message); (b) expanding fires the card's DEFERRED REHIGHLIGHT (`data-highlight-deferred`, toggle listener) which REPLACES the card DOM and detaches the Range — every settle step re-acquires a live range from the same (stable) `.chat-msg` element when `startContainer.isConnected` goes false; (c) `_scrollNestedIntoView` scrolls nested overflow ancestors on BOTH axes — vertical (max-height cards) AND horizontal (nowrap code lines; only when the match is outside the h-viewport, so wrapped text doesn't jiggle); (d) centers the outer list on the range nearest the anchor (raw-line→message isn't 1:1). It pulses a `.chat-search-flash` overlay glued to the range for ~1.2s (takes a GETTER so it follows a re-acquired range; hidden while clipped by the list or any inner scroll container); the current highlight is a solid high-contrast `::highlight(chat-search-current)` vs the dim `chat-search` and `applyHighlightLayer` re-asserts the current highlight from a stored node+offset `_currentAnchor` (scroll-driven re-applies would otherwise wipe it). Search covers the WHOLE file and STREAMS progressively (less-style live count): `searchJsonlFullStream` (codex adapter) reads the JSONL ASYNC (yields between 16MB chunks so the response flushes and other requests aren't blocked; raw-substring pre-filter → parse candidates → match extracted text; 500-match cap; 240MB ≈ 0.6s) via `?search=q&stream=1`, writing NDJSON: a `{tailStartLine,totalLines}` preamble, then one `{line, ts, role, preview}` per hit as found, then `{done,total,truncated}`. ChatSearch (`_streamFullFileSearch`) reads the stream, jumps to the FIRST hit immediately, updates the status `${idx}/${n}… searching` live, finalizes to `${idx}/${n}${truncated?'+':''}` on done, and aborts the prior stream (AbortController) on a new query. The `Cache-Control: no-transform` header makes the compression middleware skip buffering so writes flush in real time. (Non-streaming `?search=q` + sync `searchJsonlFull` kept as a fallback.) Matches carry `{line}`; all matches seek-load/teleport by absolute file `line` (no normalized index needed — the teleport model is immune to index drift). ChatSearch auto-switches to full-file streaming mode when the gap minimap is active. The MINIMAP covers the whole conversation: `scanJsonlUserTurns` (mtime-cached) streams the file once (substring pre-filter `"role":"user"` → parse ~2k candidate lines, ~1.2s for 541MB); `?fullturnmap=1` returns every user turn in TIME coordinates + file line; `ChatMinimap.renderFullExtent` positions markers by `(ts-firstTs)/(lastTs-firstTs)`, thumb tracks the visible ts span (`setVisibleTsRange`←`_reportVisibleTsRange`, which uses getBoundingClientRect for real visibility + min/max ts, and in teleport mode ignores ts past the conversation's `lastTs` — the normalizer stamps `Date.now()` on slab records lacking a timestamp, which would otherwise stretch the thumb to the recent end; live messages are also deferred while teleported so they don't leak into the history view); clicking a marker `_jumpToFileTime(ts, line)` teleports. Messages carry `srcLine` (from each record's `__line`) + DOM `data-ts`/`data-line`. NOTE: a live-growing session's tail slides forward, so tail-relative indices drift for the active session — teleport-by-line sidesteps this entirely.
- Codex resume self-referencing fork chain: newer codex keeps the SAME thread id on resume, but the spawn-time env chain appended the resume target unconditionally → `forked_from` contained the thread itself → discovery's merged-thread suppression hid the session from the list after termination. Wrapper now filters its own threadId from the emitted chain.
- Codex thread vanished from session list permanently: a transient IO error in `extractCodexThreadMeta` was swallowed and the empty meta (threadId='') was cached keyed by the file's mtime — if the session never wrote again (terminated), the entry never invalidated. Fix: failed extractions are never cached.
- Stale openSpec replay → blank chat window with outdated title: a window whose dtach session died and was resumed under a NEW server id kept `serverId`/`name` from creation time in its `_openSpec`. `replayOpenSpec` replayed them verbatim (attach to nonexistent session → blank; stale first-user-message name instead of custom rename), `captureState` dropped `backendSessionId` when the stale serverId no longer matched `_allSessions` (self-perpetuating), and the server's attach-not-found error had no `sessionId` so the ChatView couldn't correlate it. Fix: replayOpenSpec re-resolves serverId/name against the live session list by backend+backendSessionId (+ `getCustomName`), falls back to `viewSession` when dead; captureState/restoreState/loadNamed fall back to `openSpec.backendSessionId`; error carries `sessionId` and ChatView goes read-only with the Resume bar.
- Chat drag-upload overlay permanently visible ("won't disappear"): **this project has NO global `.hidden {display:none}` — every component defines its own scoped rule**. The new `.chat-drop-overlay`/`.chat-upload-toast` had a base `display:flex` and toggled a `.hidden` class with no matching CSS, so they were never hidden. Fix: added `.chat-drop-overlay.hidden`/`.chat-upload-toast.hidden { display:none }`. Verification gotcha: assert `getComputedStyle(el).display`, NOT `classList.contains('hidden')` — the class toggled correctly the whole time while the element stayed `display:flex`. (Same root cause as the earlier minimap-label-not-hiding bug.) The overlay show/hide itself uses a dragover-idle timer (no `dragleave`/`relatedTarget` — unreliable in Safari — and no `dragend`, which OS/Finder file drags never fire).
- Claude fork behaved identically to resume in chat: the WebUI **never captured Claude's stream-json `session_id`** (zero refs anywhere — for new sessions the id was filled in lazily by lock-first discovery). `--fork-session` makes claude mint a NEW session id and write a separate JSONL (verified empirically: plain resume reuses the id, fork returns a fresh one), but the server kept tracking the PARENT id passed at creation — so a forked window shadowed the original (same name/history/resume target) and the fork's transcript was orphaned. Fix: the **claude** stdout parser (`setupSessionPty`'s chat branch is `if (backend==='codex'){…} else {…claude…}` — the adoption MUST go in the `else`; a first attempt in the codex branch silently never ran) adopts `msg.session_id` when it differs from the tracked id, records the parent in `forkedFrom` (informational for Claude — discovery never hides on it, unlike Codex), persists `claudeSessionId` in session meta, and `broadcastActiveSessions()`. Guarded by a one-shot `session._forkRequested` flag (set in ws-handler only when `data.fork` + Claude) so a normal resume — whose id the parser also sees on every line — can never be hijacked. **FIRST capture is UNCONDITIONAL since 2.156.1 (lengyue real incident): the fork guard used to veto null→id adoption — the ONLY parser-side capture — so a brand-new session could never learn its id from the stream; local sessions were silently rescued by lock-first discovery, REMOTE keeper sessions were not (meta null forever → attach transcript-prefetch path error → window permanently blank while the remote claude ran fine). With no tracked id there is nothing to hijack; a CHANGED id still requires the fork flag.** **Timing gotcha (why it looks like resume at first):** under `--input-format stream-json` claude emits NOTHING until the first input message — the fork id rides in the `system/hook_started`/init line that only appears AFTER the user sends their first message. So a freshly-forked window is genuinely indistinguishable from a resume until you continue it; on that first turn claude forks, the parser adopts the new id, and the window becomes its own session (separate JSONL, distinct sidebar entry, resumes as the fork). The client propagates the adopted id to the window `_openSpec` via `syncSessionIdentity` on the next `active-sessions` broadcast (same path Codex fork/resume uses). Needs a server restart to take effect (dtach sessions survive it). Verified live: fork + one message → `backendSessionId` 649e5dbe… → 5c480868…. **UX follow-up:** because the divergence needs a first message, clicking Fork (chat mode) now opens `#dialog-fork` (a "first message" popup); submit forks AND sends it (`createSession({initialMessage})` → `_sendChatMessage` → `chat-input`, sent AFTER history renders so `loadHistory` doesn't wipe the echoed message) so the session diverges immediately instead of mimicking a resume. Terminal-mode forks skip the popup. The popup also has an editable **Title** field (`#fork-title`, pre-filled with the default `<base> (forked)` via `_defaultForkName`) so you fork straight into the title you want; the title is passed as the session name (window title is right immediately) and — once the fork's NEW id is adopted (`syncSessionIdentity`, guarded by a remembered `parentId` so the parent isn't renamed before divergence) — persisted as a custom name (`sidebar.setCustomName`) keyed by the fork's session key. The window-title resolver prefers `getCustomName`, so a forked window keeps its real title instead of falling back to the first-message-derived name after it stops or the page reloads. **Fork-from-message (point-in-time fork):** each assistant message in chat shows a GitHub repo-forked icon (`UI_ICONS.forkBranch`) next to the open-in-editor button (`addForkBtn`, claude-only, assistant-only, not subagent views, requires `msg.uuid`). It branches a session truncated at that message via `claude --resume <id> --resume-session-at <message.uuid> --fork-session`. **Two CLI gotchas (found by disassembling the binary; the help text misleads on both):** (1) `--resume-session-at`'s help says "(use with --resume **in print mode**)" but it works fine in our stream-json interactive mode — verified live, no `--print` needed (which we must never use → program-use billing). (2) help calls the arg `<message id>` but it's looked up by **`message.uuid`** (the JSONL record uuid), NOT `message.id` (`msg_…`) — passing the latter errors `No message found with message.uuid of …`. So the normalizer now threads the raw `uuid` onto every message (next to `srcLine`). The forked window's displayed history is truncated to match via `/api/session-messages?untilUuid=<uuid>` (returns the convo up to that message, last 50 of that range, `total=upto` so scroll-up still paginates). Related discovered-but-unused: `--rewind-files <user-message-id>` restores **file** state to a message point (the rewind/checkpoint feature — separate from conversation fork). Verified live end-to-end: fork-at + message → new id adopted (2a1e29c6…).
- Minimap/search accuracy (huge sessions, reconnect, gap slabs) — five related fixes, keep ALL of them: (1) index→element mapping must use `'.chat-msg:not(.chat-gap-msg)'` — gap-loaded elements are in the DOM but OUTSIDE the window index space, so a bare `.chat-msg` NodeList misaligns `relIdx` onto the wrong message (search expanded/scrolled the wrong card once any gap slab was loaded). (2) `_reattach` catch-up must advance `_windowEnd` after appending missed messages (`_fetchMessages` silently updates `_total` via `_fetchMessagePage`, so the two diverge otherwise — post-reconnect minimap thumb/pos-indicator/jumps were off by the missed count); it also feeds missed user turns to the minimap and re-applies the search highlight. (3) The search highlight layer must be re-applied after EVERY window mutation: `_extendTop` AND `_extendBottom`/`jumpToIndex`/`jumpToBottom` (only the first did → highlights vanished scrolling down). (4) Full-extent (time-coordinate) minimap: live messages have ts beyond the init-time `lastTs` — `updateThumb` clamps against `max(lastTs, visibleBotTs)` (stale span pinned the thumb to top:100%, overflowing the track) and new live user turns call `appendFullTurn`. (5) Index-mode markers are `startIdx/total` — `setViewport` repositions them when total changes; edit re-renders must preserve `dataset.ts` (create path sets it, the edit path lost it).
- CodeMirror active-line highlight hid the selection on the first/last selected line: `highlightActiveLine` (from `basicSetup`) decorates the line under the selection HEAD even during a range selection, and that background paints on `.cm-line` ABOVE the selection layer (`z-index:-1`), so the opaque light-theme active-line (`#f1f5f9`) covered the selection rect on that one line. Fix: tag the editor `.cm-has-selection` when any range is non-empty + a theme rule `&.cm-has-selection .cm-activeLine{background:transparent}` (outranks light + oneDark `.cm-activeLine`). **Focus gotcha:** first attempt toggled the class directly on `view.dom` via a ViewPlugin — but CodeMirror rebuilds `view.dom.className` from scratch on every focus change (`updateAttrs` → `"cm-editor" + (cm-focused) + themeClasses`), wiping the class, so the highlight reappeared once the editor lost focus. Correct way: contribute the class through the **`EditorView.editorAttributes` facet** (a function value) — `attrsFromFacet` re-evaluates it on every update (incl. selection + focus, `updateAttrs` runs at the end of each view update) and `combineAttrs` CONCATENATES its class into the className CM builds, so it survives blur. Both editors share `activeLineSelectionPatch` (exported from code-editor.js). Lesson: never mutate `view.dom.classList` on a CodeMirror editor — it's clobbered on focus/theme changes; use the editorAttributes facet.
